Eden May Arrive in Czech Capital This Morning; No Development in British-Polish Talks; Met with Pilsudski for a Long Talk Lasting Fifty Minutes; Conditions for Poland to Join the Eastern European Pact Must Be Considered 41

Warsaw After Eden met with Polish Foreign Minister Beck and President Mościcki today, he had another meeting with Army Chief Pilsudski for fifty minutes. The meeting took place at the Belvedere Palace. Both spoke in French. Pilsudski clarified Poland's position, especially regarding the Eastern European Military Mutual Assistance Pact. There were no new decisions made in today's talks. However, it is believed that various suggestions were considered, and it is expected that French Foreign Minister Laval's visit to Warsaw in the future will influence the future development of Poland's foreign policy. Poland has so far opposed all suggestions for the Eastern European Pact. Its final decision on this matter has a significant impact on the Anglo-French proposal of February 3, as it includes this pact. According to various newspapers, Poland seems to indicate its attitude before Eden leaves tomorrow. However, the conditions for its accession to the Pact must be carefully considered at the London or Stresa Conference. This condition was anticipated at the beginning of Eden's departure, and at that time it was clearly stated that all the information collected in the capitals would be thoroughly studied after Eden returned home. Tonight, Beck's dinner party for Eden was well attended by Polish officials and their wives. Beck gave a speech welcoming Eden, saying that the Polish people deeply appreciated the British government's goodwill in seeking to promote international relations and consolidate mutual trust. Poland is willing to cooperate. Eden replied that he believed that this trip would enable closer understanding between Britain and Poland. Both countries' policies are based on the principle of collective security and rely on the League of Nations. He believed that the very friendly talks made by both sides were very valuable because they could enable them to understand their obligations in the great work of international peace organization. (Reuters telegram on the 3rd)

Warsaw Minister Chang-er Eden declared that before leaving Warsaw this afternoon, he will also hold talks with the diplomatic representatives of France, Italy, and Czechoslovakia in Poland. This morning, Eden and Polish Foreign Minister Burke held their third meeting. He can arrive in the Czech capital tomorrow morning and hold talks with Czech Foreign Minister Beneš. The next day, he will return home by plane. By Friday, he will report the results of his visits to Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia to the cabinet in detail. So far, there has been no concrete development in the situation. A certain British official told the reporter of this agency, "The United Kingdom will ultimately believe that if the United Kingdom is unwilling to be a mediator and directly bear its responsibilities, then lasting peace in Europe will be impossible. However, in exchange, the countries of the European continent must also guarantee to the United Kingdom that neither the United Kingdom nor its territories will accept special restrictions on any particular area of Europe. In short, all problems are only in finding a formula for peace in Europe." In addition, British officials believe that the final solution will not go beyond two types. One is to have France and the Eastern European countries sign the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, excluding Germany and Poland, but allowing Germany and Poland to join in the future. The other is to conclude a broader pact that includes all European countries, including the United Kingdom. (Havas telegram on the 3rd)

Warsaw Any compromise suggestions regarding the Eastern European Locarno Pact that Polish Foreign Minister Beck may have accepted during his talks with Eden are now believed to have been dismissed by Polish dictator General Pilsudski. Eden's talks with Beck ended at noon today. Eden will depart for Prague, the capital of the Czech Republic, tonight and will discuss the general situation in Europe with Czech diplomats tomorrow morning. He is scheduled to fly back to London tomorrow afternoon. On Friday, he will report the results of his consultations with Russia, Poland, and the Czech Republic to the Cabinet. After Eden's meeting with Beck was over, the Polish authorities issued the following communiqué: Mr. Eden has given a detailed account of the exchange of views between the United Kingdom and Germany. In a harmonious discussion, the Foreign Minister briefly outlined Poland's views on the matters listed in the London communiqué of February 3 and on the general situation in Europe. Both sides agreed that this exchange of views was purely exploratory and had satisfactorily achieved its purpose. (Reuters telegram on the 3rd)

Eden Proposes a Pan-European Pact

Warsaw Colonel Burke, Minister of Foreign Affairs, hosted a banquet tonight to welcome the British Lord Privy Seal Eden and the British delegation, and Burke gave a brief speech welcoming the guests, which was answered by Eden. According to the most reliable sources, Eden, because Poland seems unwilling to abandon its position between Germany and Russia and join the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, will propose a mutual assistance pact be concluded by all European countries, including the United Kingdom, on the condition that armaments are substantially reduced. Eden had two meetings with Burke this morning and afternoon, and visited General Pilsudski, Minister of Military and Political Affairs, in the evening. (Havas telegram on the 2nd)

Warsaw It is believed in Polish official circles that Germany does not intend to participate in the Eastern European Pact under the current circumstances, so Poland cannot participate immediately. This news is said to have been issued after the meeting between the British Lord Privy Seal Eden and Polish Foreign Minister Beck. It is also learned that Poland is quite willing to participate in and cooperate with any peace movement, but because Poland is located in a vital area between Russia and Germany, it is particularly unwilling to sign the existing form of the Pact. It is said that what Beck opposes is the point that Germany will be rejected if it is unwilling to participate. Because of this, the result will be that Germany will be encircled. It is likely that Germany will not agree to the pact currently under discussion, so Polish official circles hope to modify it, and Poland must wait until after the modification before deciding what to do. At the same time, Eden is still continuing meetings with Beck. French Foreign Minister Laval also plans to stay in Warsaw for several days when he sets out for Russia to participate in the discussion. Observers say that regardless of whether the Eastern European Pact is established or not, Laval will probably make a concrete proposal for a Franco-Russian military alliance to the Soviet Union. (National News Agency telegram on the 3rd)

Signs of Anglo-Russian Rapprochement Have Emerged

(London) Members of the British Parliament have a very favorable attitude towards the results of the talks between the United Kingdom and Russia. In general, signs of Anglo-Russian rapprochement have emerged, and it will not cause fierce opposition from the Conservative Party. The fact that the House of Commons is not eager to ask the government to explain the situation of the Moscow talks shows that the majority party has expressed goodwill towards the Anglo-Russian talks. (Havas telegram on the 2nd)

(London) The Morning Post commented on Lord Privy Seal Eden's trip to Eastern Europe, saying, "People all over the world hope that Germany will realize that isolation is not a good plan and join the Eastern European Pact. Sooner or later, it does not matter. Therefore, the door to compromise must not be blocked. However, if Germany hesitates outside the door after all, the way to ensure peace is to unite the strength of other countries so that Germany does not dare to provoke." The Daily Telegraph said, "It is becoming increasingly clear that the Eastern European security problem cannot be solved by concluding regional agreements." The Daily Mail said, "Eden's trip was purely exploratory and failed to break the deadlock. It is not Eden's fault. It is hoped that French Foreign Minister Laval's trip to Eastern Europe will be successful." (Havas telegram on the 3rd)

It Is Difficult to Expect Approval for Germany's Proposal

(London) It is now learned that when German leader Hitler spoke with British Foreign Minister Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden in Berlin last week, he put forward a method to replace the Eastern European Pact. It is said that this proposal is to reiterate the theory of concluding non-aggression pacts separately, with the addition of clauses on ceasing assistance and supply to aggressor countries. This kind of pact can eventually be included in a multi-faceted non-aggression pact. However, according to the opinion of Reuters' diplomatic correspondent, this method may not be approved by France and Russia, because France and Russia are both members of the League of Nations, and according to the Kellogg Pact, which declares that it does not use war as an instrument of national policy, they have already assumed non-aggression. What Germany proposed is also not as thorough as Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, because this article stipulates that any country engaged in war should be regarded as an act of war against other members of the League of Nations, and other members will immediately sever all commercial and financial relations with it. In any case, France and Russia, who advocate the Eastern European Pact, will inevitably say that the existing non-aggression method is not enough to guarantee security. (Reuters telegram on the 2nd)

Press Comments on the Three-Four Conference

(London) The Italian Popolo d'Italia published a commentary today, stating that at the upcoming Stresa Conference, the United Kingdom, France, and Italy should specifically state that they hold a common view, and must further determine a common action program to deal with certain definite situations. People here believe that this commentary in the Italian Popolo d'Italia should be due to the instructions of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, so it is quite impressive. All the evening newspapers reprinted a summary of the article today. Political figures expressed that if the United Kingdom, France, and Italy can hold a unified view at the Stresa Conference, it would be a great wish, but the United Kingdom does not hope to take a definite attitude towards Germany in advance. If so, Berlin will regard it as Britain's hostility towards Germany. As for the pacts to guarantee Austria's independence and the Eastern European Pact, the extent to which the United Kingdom can participate seems to be only within the scope of consultation. (Havas telegram on the 2nd)

Another Dispute Between Italy and Abyssinia; Abyssinian Embassy in Britain Issues Statement 42

(London) The Abyssinian Embassy in Britain recently declared to the Daily Telegraph that the incident that occurred on the border between Italian Eritrea and Abyssinia on March 23 was a trap set by Italian troops. French Prime Minister's Declaration in the Chamber of Deputies: Strengthen National Defense and Expand Armaments; Plans to Conclude Military Agreements and Maintain the Gold Standard; Chamber of Deputies Passes Vote of Confidence in the Government by a Majority 43

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies held its last meeting today before the holiday. Prime Minister Flandin attended and delivered a general policy statement. After that, the Chamber of Deputies announced its adjournment until it reopened on May 28. Flandin's declaration first stated that before Germany restored conscription, it had already established a compulsory labor system, the nature of which was no different from conscription. As for Germany's announcement of forming 36 army divisions, it has not yet included the air force and artillery. Under these circumstances, France has no choice but to take appropriate steps to increase national defense and must conclude military agreements with other countries that aim to maintain peace. In addition to strengthening border defenses, France will convene a Supreme National Defense Conference on April 5 to decide to continue training the new recruits who are due to be discharged this month to prevent accidents. If this matter is decided, the French standing army can be increased by 160,000 people. As for the previously passed bill to extend the term of military service, its purpose is only to supplement the standing army quota for the "gap year," which is temporary in nature. Now that Germany has restored conscription, as soon as the German military system is finally determined, the French military system must be re-examined before it can be said to be complete. Flandin then stated the situation of the treasury, saying that France's finances are completely sound and the gold standard can be maintained to the end. Finally, he said that France has applied to the Executive Council of the League of Nations to deal with Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles, hoping that the national debate will cooperate with the government more widely to provide diplomatic backing. After Flandin finished his speech, the Chamber of Deputies passed a vote of confidence in the government by a large majority of 410 votes to 134. (Paris telegram on the 2nd)

(London) Minister of Aviation Tailon detailed the government's plan to strengthen the air force at the Air Defense Conference today, saying that the government plans to triple the tonnage of French bombers in the shortest possible time, double their range, and include all necessary purposes. Even in peacetime, the sky must be constantly defended. A team of the world's most modern pursuit aircraft will soon be established, equipped with the most sophisticated artillery. Heavy aircraft can now fly about 600 miles in one go. The government is now working hard to complete this task as soon as possible and will never slacken off. (Reuters telegram on the 2nd)

(London) Prime Minister Flandin's declaration in the Chamber of Deputies yesterday received overwhelming support. The newspapers expressed great satisfaction with it. Even the right-wing newspapers, which had adopted a reserved attitude towards Flandin for some time, now expressed sympathy. The newspapers believed that the government's authority would inevitably be expanded on the eve of the important international talks. Le Petit Parisien stated, "A summary of a policy should be done at any time, without having to make a fuss about it. It is satisfying that the French people can maintain a calm mind and have an unwavering belief in the future of the country." (Havas telegram on the 3rd)

US Senate Arms Committee Cancels War Profits Plan; Limits War Profiteering by Arms Dealers 48

(Washington) The Senate Arms Committee today completed its plan to eliminate war profits and will submit a report to the Senate. The plan includes the conscription of industry and manpower during wartime and a limit on individual income to no more than 10,000 yuan per year. The chairman of the committee is Progressive Republican Senator Nye. The report to be submitted this time is the most radical proposal in the US Congress. Although Nye had several conflicts with President Roosevelt during the investigation of the arms trade, it is said that the President has approved the plan to eliminate wartime profiteering and has declared that the magnitude of wartime profits is indescribable, especially for arms manufacturers, and that such profits should be thoroughly eliminated. However, some arms dealers are cooperating with the government, so if the Arms Committee wants its plan to pass, it may not have any other strong proposals besides suggesting that the government directly control all arms manufacturing plants. The President also strongly criticized the injustice of soldiers fighting abroad during the European War only receiving one yuan per day, while workers in the rear could earn eight to twenty yuan per day. Reactionary elements in Congress may oppose this plan, arguing that the poor performance of state-owned railways is an example of the ineffectiveness of state control compared to private management. (National Telegraph, 2nd)

(Washington) The Senate Arms Committee passed a bill late today stipulating that the state shall bear all the expenses of future wars to avoid burdening future generations. The bill was drafted by Nye, chairman of the Arms Committee. It will require the government to register the board of directors of major industries and treat them with the salary of a major general, about 8,000 yuan per year. According to the bill, the government will not be able to directly manage the arms industry, but it will control profits during wartime and force directors to take responsibility for the front line with their usual management skills. It is said that the latter clause can greatly alleviate the opposition of conservatives, because they stated that the government's takeover of the railways during the Great War was clear proof of the government's inability to manage private enterprises. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

Case of German Journalist Lured and Kidnapped; Switzerland Will Report to the World Court and Prepare to Apply for League of Nations Handling 49

Bern The kidnapping of German Overseas Chinese journalist Jakob, who was hiding in Basel, by the National Socialist Party has caused a national uproar, recognizing this as undermining Swiss sovereignty. Foreign Minister Motta read to the Parliament a copy of the note requesting Germany to return Jakob, his attitude was very indignant. This note has already been delivered to Germany. Jakob was arrested for leaking German military secrets and is now awaiting trial in a National Socialist prison, where he may be sentenced to death. Foreign Minister Motta declared that the kidnapping seriously damaged Swiss sovereignty and was enough to completely shake the fate of Switzerland. When the Swiss ambassador protested the National Socialist Party's actions on Saturday, German Foreign Minister Neurath opposed the return of Jakob, also claiming that the people of Basel recognized Weissmann as the instigator of Jakob's kidnapping and as the leader of the National Socialist secret organization "Gestapo." The purpose of organizing the Gestapo is to detect the actions of National Socialist Party fugitives throughout Europe. Moreover, Weissmann has admitted that on March 9, he lured Jakob from his hiding place in Switzerland and then handed him over to a National Socialist envoy, who transported him back to Germany in a high-speed car. Motta finally stated that he would report the matter to the World Court. It is now known that the government is preparing to apply to the League of Nations to handle the case. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

Siam Expands Navy; Stipulates Huge Expenses for Building New Warships 50

Bangkok When the Siamese government's naval bill was discussed in parliament today, the opposition party criticized the government for squandering national funds, but after a long debate, the bill was finally passed. The government was victorious. The bill stipulates the construction of new warships at a cost of 1.75 million pounds, to be paid over six years. The Siamese navy is the smallest in the world, with only three gunboats, three destroyers, and three torpedo boats, and some other small warships. The active-duty Siamese navy personnel total 4,800, with 20,000 reservists. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Lord Peel Advocates That Britain Mediate Sino-Japanese Relations; Assuming Role of Mediator to Seek an Agreement; Raising the Issue of the Far East for Government Attention in the House of Lords 51

(London) Lord Peel will raise a motion in the House of Lords at 4 pm today, requesting the government to pay attention to the situation in the Far East and Sino-Japanese relations. A debate is expected. Eddington and others will speak for the government, and Lords Reading and Lytton will also likely express their opinions. Opposition peers will pay attention to the trend of the debate, and Lord Marley will be promoted to speak when necessary. It is generally believed that the mover, Lord Peel, advocates that Britain, in view of its far-reaching interests in China, its long-standing relationship with China, and its friendly relations with both China and Japan, should immediately try to assume the role of mediator between China and Japan to seek an agreement that can eliminate Chinese suspicions of Japanese intentions and enable China to carry out its economic development along its existing borders. Peel will also urge Britain to guarantee Japan its due position in the Chinese market and other satisfactory matters, so as to be in line with its special position in the Far East. Observers familiar with the situation in the Far East believe that Britain is best qualified to undertake such work, because Britain's motives are beyond doubt. If a meeting of the signatory countries of the Nine-Power Treaty is convened, it will inevitably resemble a trial of Japan, which will only vent hatred and be harmful to a peace agreement. If China and Japan conclude an agreement themselves, it may arouse deeper suspicions among overseas Chinese. Today's debate in the House of Lords will likely involve negotiations on loans to China, but according to observers, the first priority is to eliminate the shadows of suspicion and hatred that shroud the Far East. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

Japanese Economic Policy Towards China Brought by the Roving Business Official; Opposes Britain's Proposal to Send an Investigation Team; Prepares to Consider Loans for China's Self-Reliance 52

(Tokyo) Horitake Heitaro, the commercial counselor stationed in China, who has been conferring with Foreign Minister Hirota and various parties since returning to Japan, is scheduled to take the Nagasaki Maru from Kobe to Shanghai on April 4 to return to his post. The foreign ministry authorities have instructed him on the following general economic policy toward China: 1. There is no other way to rescue the Chinese economy except to wait for self-reliance. Therefore, if China itself drafts a concrete plan for self-reliance, Japan is also prepared to consider loans if they are necessary for implementation. However, loans for military or other non-productive purposes are of no benefit to China itself. Therefore, even if other countries intend to provide loans, Japan will resolutely oppose them. 2. The proposal to send a survey team by various countries, as proposed by Britain, to investigate China's economic situation is also absolutely opposed. 3. Japan will purchase Chinese cotton and other agricultural products in large quantities, and in order to promote such production, Japan is prepared to provide technical assistance. Minister Zhang to Poland Liaises with Literary and Artistic Circles; China's Protest Against Partition of Poland Still Archived in Soviet Russian National Library 92

Poland Dispatch: Zhang Xinhai, the minister to Poland, and his wife, Han Xiangmei, who has taught for many years, are Western literature scholars in the country. After being dispatched overseas during the European war, he was transferred from Portugal to Poland, where he received a warm welcome from the Polish literary and artistic circles. It is reported that recently, the philosopher Lutoslawski, who has long admired Minister Zhang's reputation, despite being over seventy years old, came from Krakow to Warsaw to visit him and hold long-term discussions on Chinese and Western philosophy. He also invited Minister Zhang to give a lecture at the University of Krakow. Furthermore, Ossendowski, the president of the Polish Literary Society, also invited Minister Zhang to give a lecture. This year marks the 1400th anniversary of Tao Yuanming's death. Minister Zhang plans to lecture on Tao's poetry and introduce Tao's works to the Polish people. Additionally, the Polish historian Askenazy visited Minister Zhang and discussed how during the reign of Emperor Qianlong of the Qing Dynasty, Russia, Germany, and Austria partitioned Poland. Emperor Qianlong protested to Russia, stating that the partition of Poland was the most shameful event in history. Emperor Qianlong spoke out of righteousness, which the Polish people still remember. The original protest document is still archived in a certain library in Soviet Russia. Mr. Askenazy offered a Russian translation. This is an interesting historical material of China's heyday, which can be used as reference for people in the country.

Newly Organized Security Force Soon to Enter War Zone; Yin Tao Arrives in Tianjin for Negotiations, Japanese Side Fully Agrees 93

Beiping Dispatch: The issue of rotating the "war zone" security force has been brewing for almost a year. Due to numerous entanglements, the implementation procedures are quite complicated. After the issue of transferring the security force of Yutian County, led by Feng Shoupeng, was resolved, the cleaning work in the "war zone" has gained momentum and is progressing smoothly. The matter of the newly organized security force entering the "war zone" is also nearing fruition. The deployment date can be determined in Tianjin tonight (the 2nd). Here is what we have heard:

Tianjin Meeting

During a plenary meeting of the "War Zone Cleanup Committee" last month, resolutions were passed. Yin Tong, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, and Tao Shangming, the commissioner of the Luan-Yu area, arrived in Tianjin at the end of last month and held separate negotiations with representatives of the provincial government and the Japanese side, including Goujin and Ii. They have reached full agreement on the deployment of the newly organized security force. The provincial government has also telegraphed Zhang Yantian and Zhang Qingyu, the commanders of the first and second regiments of the newly organized security force, to come to Tianjin to discuss everything.

Seeking Instructions from He

Yin Rugeng, the commissioner of the Ji-Mi area, remained in Beiping to arrange the implementation work. This morning (the 2nd) at 9:00 AM, he went to Jurentang to meet with He Yingqin. In addition to reporting on the transfer of the Yutian security force and the thorough reorganization of illegal militias, he also gave a detailed account of the recent work of the "War Zone Cleanup Committee." Subsequently, he sought instructions on all matters concerning the deployment of the newly organized security force. He gave detailed instructions. Yin left around 11:00 AM and immediately took the Ping-Yu express train departing from Beiping at 1:15 PM to Tianjin.

Banquet at Ning Garden

Yin Tong held a banquet at Beining Park this afternoon (the 2nd) at 7:00 PM. Yin Rugeng, Tao Shangming, Zhang Yantian, and Zhang Qingyu attended. Zhu Shiqin, a section chief of the Military Affairs Commission, was also invited but did not attend due to official business. According to reliable sources, Yin Tao and others will finalize the deployment date of the newly organized security force at the banquet in Ning Garden. After the date is set, preparations for the deployment, such as vehicle scheduling, deployment routes, and the allocation of personnel and weapons, will be discussed in accordance with the agreement with the Japanese side.

Prior Inspection

Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming have tentatively scheduled to go to Beicang and Caicun on the 4th or 6th of this month to inspect the new security force. Representatives from the provincial government will also participate. During the inspection, speeches will be given to encourage them. After the inspection, preparations for the move will begin. The first regiment, led by Zhang Yantian, is currently stationed in Beicang. In the future, they will take a special train on the Beining Railway from their current location to various stations along the Ji-Yu area, and then transfer to automobiles to reach their destinations in various counties. The number of personnel is 2,500. The second regiment, led by Zhang Qingyu, is stationed in Caicun, and their number of personnel is also 2,500. In the future, they will transfer from Beiping to various counties in the Luan-Mi area. However, due to insufficient vehicles, except for the more distant counties, which will travel by automobile, the rest will march on foot.

Yin Rugeng's Talk

According to Yin Rugeng, the commissioner of the Ji-Mi area, who spoke to reporters this morning (the 2nd) after meeting with He Yingqin, he sought instructions. After the deployment of the newly organized security force is completed in the future, there will be much reorganization work within the "war zone." The so-called reorganization is purely internal, such as the reorganization of the militias in each county and the reorganization of the public security bureaus in each county, which are all urgent tasks. Without this, the security within the "war zone" will be difficult to improve. Secondly, the cleanup in Yutian County and the anti-banditry work after the green crops appear are also things that should be done. Only after everything in the "war zone" is on track can construction be discussed. The issue of receiving Leling will be carried out after the above matters are completed step by step. It is believed that in the foreseeable future, the cleanup work in the "war zone" can come to an end. (February 2nd)

Qingdao Citizens' Thrift and Savings Campaign; The Purpose of Thrift and Savings Is Not Only for Individuals, But Also to Increase National Productivity 94

Qingdao Correspondence: Since the establishment of the preparatory committee for the city's thrift and savings campaign, it has held several meetings, and successively passed the campaign plan, the organizational outline of the thrift alliance, and the campaign declaration. Mayor Shen Honglie was specially appointed as the honorary president, Secretary-General Hu Jiafeng as the president, and the heads of various bureaus and stations as the vice presidents. The opening ceremony was held at the YMCA at 3:00 PM on March 31, with more than a hundred representatives from all walks of life attending. The meeting was extremely enthusiastic. The campaign lasted for a week, with famous people invited to give lectures every night, and lecture groups also went to the city and suburbs during the day to explain the meaning of thrift and savings to persuade people. The grand opening and the organizational outline of the thrift alliance are recorded as follows:

Grand Opening

After the ceremony, Chairman Lin Fengqi gave the opening speech, stating that it is a good phenomenon that the citizens of this city are promoting the thrift campaign under the current environment. The purpose of thrift and savings is not only for individuals, but mainly to increase national productivity, enrich the national economy, and is extremely important for the future of the country. He expressed his gratitude to Mayor Shen and other officials for their guidance and expressed his expectation that there would be new progress within this week. Next, Mayor Shen gave a speech, stating that he was very interested in attending the opening ceremony of the thrift and savings campaign today. When he was in the navy, he also promoted diligence and thrift, and specially established the Diligence and Aspiration Society, which all soldiers joined. Every month, in addition to personal expenses and supporting their families, all the remaining money was saved. Later, because he was busy, he could not take care of it, and the matter failed. After he became the mayor, he still did not slack off in this matter, established the Diligence and Improvement Association, and established supply and entertainment clubs to promote noble entertainment for civil servants, hoping to cultivate good habits, but unfortunately the results were still minimal. There are two reasons for the failure: first, because this matter was mostly passive, it could not last, and there was no joint organization, it was easily moved by the environment; second, because the national character of our country is loose, individuals have no plans. Because he learned from the failures of the past, he only focused on the actual situation of his subordinates and promoted the "three no's and three yes's" doctrine. The three no's are: no whoring, no gambling, no drug abuse; the three yes's are: yes to reading, yes to exercise, yes to cooperation. The thrift and savings campaign promoted by the YMCA is in line with his intentions. Therefore, he is interested in this matter. He described the failures of the past in order to study the rescue methods for this matter and make sure to get good results. Rescue methods can be divided into two aspects, the official aspect can be divided into broad and narrow. The broad sense belongs to education, such as promoting reading, exercise, noble entertainment, etc., making them have the spirit of getting rid of bad habits, cultivating good habits, and good learning. The narrow sense belongs to material, in the future, the city government civil servants will also imitate other methods to be frugal and thrifty in order to save money, and promote frugality and thrift by example. The two aspects, the official aspect and the people's aspect, must work hard to promote. The people should increase production as much as possible and create wealth to meet the needs of society. Merchants should take the overall situation into consideration and not sell foreign goods, so as to prevent leaks. In Qingdao, merchants are more important than farmers and workers. In a narrow sense, it is thrift and savings. However, it is not difficult to carry out thrift campaigns among farmers and workers, because farmers and workers are usually very frugal and do not wait to be persuaded. What is difficult is the intellectual class. The YMCA has initiated this meeting, and most of the participants are intellectuals. In the future, it is hoped that all the intellectuals in the city will be gathered together, and various methods will be used to unite them. Do not just talk about this matter, but practice it, then the future of the country may be hopeful. After the speech, Hu Jiafeng, the chairman, and Li Shiliao, the standing committee member of the city party department, gave speeches successively, and then took pictures and adjourned the meeting.

Alliance Outline

The purpose of this alliance is to promote personal thrift and savings, eliminate various wasteful habits in material and spirit, and thus improve economic life. Anyone who agrees with the purpose of this alliance and is willing to practice it can join as a basic ally. The allies of this alliance are divided into groups of ten people, and are numbered from the first group to the nth group in the order of their establishment. (Each group pushes one representative to organize a representative assembly as the highest authority. Each ally must introduce at least ten people to form a group. This alliance has a number of promotion committee members who organize a promotion committee to lead the worship of the alliance under the guidance of the group representative assembly. The first promotion committee is organized by the basic allies, and the second and subsequent committees are organized by the group representative assembly. The term of office of the group representatives and promotion committee members is one year, and they can be re-elected. Allies must abide by the alliance agreement in their personal life and in their interactions with other allies. The alliance agreement will be determined separately. Separate saving methods will be implemented for public life, banquets, gift-giving, and holidays. This alliance can establish special agreements with savings institutions, insurance institutions, and other stores to facilitate the allies. Various detailed rules for the promotion committee and the group of ten people will be determined separately. This outline will be implemented after being approved by the general meeting of basic allies. If there are any unfulfilled matters, it can be revised by the group representative assembly.

Alliance Covenant

Be punctual and strictly observe the agreed time. Be frugal with clothing, try to reduce the manufacture of new clothes, and use domestic products as much as possible. Be frugal with food, do not eat between meals, do not engage in useless socializing, and do not eat expensive things. Be frugal with expenses, do not waste, do not visit prostitutes, do not gamble, and do not use drugs. If there are others such as not smoking cigarettes, not drinking alcohol, not engaging in speculative businesses, not dancing, and not purchasing unnecessary items, the small group can formulate special agreements to be jointly observed. If anyone violates this alliance covenant or harms the reputation of this alliance, and does not change after being advised by the promotion committee, they should withdraw from the alliance immediately and be announced as withdrawn.

Japan's Siwen Society Invites Descendants of Sages to Japan to Participate in the Completion Ceremony of the Confucius Temple; Provincial Government Will Select Representatives to Attend 95

Jinan Dispatch: Japan's Siwen Society, in order to rebuild the Yushima Confucius Temple, has set the completion ceremony to be held in Tokyo on the 28th of this month. Because Confucius was a native of Lu, and the descendants of the four sages, Yan Hui, Zeng Shen, Zisi, and Mencius, are mostly in Shandong, they have specially invited Kong Decheng, the official in charge of the worship of Confucius, Kong Lingcan, a descendant of Confucius, one descendant of each of the four sages, and famous people from various places to participate. The Japanese consul in Jinan, Nishida, has asked the provincial authorities for permission to go. If the direct descendants of the sages cannot participate in person, they are requested to send one representative each. The authorities, considering this matter to be of great importance, have requested instructions from the central government. Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan telegraphed Lu on the 26th of last month. On the 30th, the authorities received telegrams from the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, stating that the candidates for the descendants of the sages and Confucian scholars should be selected by the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Education, and their resumes should be submitted to the ministry for approval. The Shandong Provincial Government believes that the candidates for the descendants of each sage should be selected by the Department of Education and the Department of Civil Affairs, and one or two experienced representatives of the sages with diplomatic knowledge, and two to four representatives of Confucian scholars, should be selected and their resumes should be submitted to the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education for joint approval. This was resolved at the provincial administrative meeting today (the 2nd), and the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Education were ordered to handle it accordingly. It is reported that Kong Decheng, the official in charge of the worship of Confucius, and Kong Lingcan, a descendant of Confucius, have decided not to participate in person. As for the descendants of the four sages, except for Zisi, who is directly related to Confucius, and Zeng Shen, who will not send anyone to participate, Yan and Mencius will be allowed to send representatives to Japan to participate. It is likely that no Confucian scholars will go. The descendants of each sage are currently studying the selection of representatives. After the provincial government selects them, they will go to Beijing to receive instructions before going to Japan. (2nd)

Boundary Dispute Between Guangdong and Guangxi Resolved; Two Provinces Send Commissioners to Survey and Agree on Two Methods of Demarcation 96

Guangzhou Correspondence: The boundary between Qin County in the southern part of Guangdong Province and Yong County in Guangxi Province is contiguous. Recently, boundary disputes have occurred in border villages, and the situation is deadlocked. The county governments of each county have submitted reports to their superiors for handling. The provincial governments of the two provinces sent officials to survey the boundary to resolve the disputes. Recently, Hu Jixian, a member of the Guangdong Provincial Government, and Lei Yin, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs of Guangxi Province, were ordered to go to the border area between Qin and Yong to inspect. The results of the meeting are as follows: It is found that the county chronicles of the two counties are different, and the surveys by the two provinces last year were inconsistent. Recently, the reports from both sides are also different. In order to thoroughly resolve this, the Southwest Political Affairs Council will send members to lead two surveying members from each province to remeasure the boundary between the two counties and the location of nearby cities and villages, so as to solve the problem once and for all. Before the Southwest Political Affairs Council approves the boundary line, everything should remain as it is, and neither side should create trouble. The county magistrates of the two counties should be responsible for instructing the township heads in their jurisdictions to guarantee that there will be no armed conflicts and that various transportation projects will not be hindered or damaged. The seventeen villages of the Qin nationality in the Sanguan area of Yong County are too far from the Qin County government, and its reach is too short. Qin County can send officials to be stationed there permanently to be responsible for managing the people there in regards to smoking, gambling, theft, smuggling, tax evasion, and other matters, and cooperate with the Yongning County government to take consistent actions. It is not necessary to plan to establish a market near Chenna in the seventeen villages, as it will only increase the resentment of the residents of Chenna. It should be stopped to resolve the dispute and wait quietly for a solution. The regulations on the establishment of markets and traffic and education in the bandit areas interspersed between the two provinces are as follows: Within ten miles of the original market, the people of the two provinces shall not establish another market. When establishing a new market more than ten miles away from the original market, the following conditions must be met: First, the market days must not be the same. Second, all taxes and fees in the newly established market, such as taxes on slaughtering pigs, cattle, tobacco, alcohol, stamp duty, and business tax, must be handled in accordance with the county's jurisdiction, and the tax rate must be the same. Third, with regard to the management of smoking, gambling, theft, smuggling, and tax evasion in the market, we should cooperate with the county government to take consistent actions. The construction of telephone lines is for the convenience of traffic, and no one shall object to or damage it on any pretext. With regard to highways, if they are provincial roads in the two provinces, they should be handled by the provincial governments of both provinces through consultation. If they are county roads and township roads, they should be handled by the county governments of both provinces through consultation. The people shall not object on any pretext. As for the township roads in the county, if they pass through the interspersed bandit area after being approved by the county government, the people along the line in the interspersed bandit area shall not object to or damage them on any pretext. With regard to educational matters, if the people in the interspersed bandit area cannot set up schools independently, they can send their children to nearby schools, but they should bear the same obligations as the local people with regard to the construction equipment of the school and the expenses of the school. Guangxi Province has telegraphed its approval of the above measures and requested that the Guangdong government sign it jointly. The original telegram said, "Regarding the dispute over the boundary between Chenna Market in Yong and Qin Counties, Commissioner Hu Jixian of your government arrived in Yong, and this government sent Commissioner Lei Yin to inspect the market together. Commissioner Hu and Commissioner Lei signed two methods, one is to demarcate the boundary between the two sides, and the other is to stipulate the methods for maintaining the boundary in the future. This government considers it to be appropriate. In addition to keeping one copy, Commissioner Hu took the remaining copy back to be submitted for approval. It is hoped that your government will approve it, and the people of the two provinces will benefit greatly." (March 30)

Songjiang Fire Brigade Members Reinstated 97

The fire brigade members of this county, because Yao and Li, two comrades, were wronged, aroused public outrage and submitted a total resignation, handing over the fire fighting equipment in each district to the Fire Association to show their determination. This has been reported in previous newspapers. After this case occurred, County Magistrate Jin, Wang, the Standing Committee member of the Party Department, District Chief Li, and Cai, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, considering the importance of fire fighting in Kailing City, invited responsible representatives from each district to the County Chamber of Commerce last night and sincerely requested their reinstatement. It took several hours to conclude. The District Public Office of the Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to the citizens, stating that Yao and Li, two members of the fire brigade, were suddenly accused in the Songhu Villa incident and were given a suspended sentence by the Shanghai District Court. The County Party Department and the County Government considered the importance of local fire fighting and invited members of the fire brigades in each district, Wang, the Standing Committee member, County Magistrate Jin, Cai, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and District Chief Li, to persuade them again and again. The members said that the fire brigade comrades originally served the local public interest. Yao and Li, two members of the fire brigade, were unjustly wronged and sentenced. They were disheartened and unwilling to sacrifice their spirit and work hard for something that was unrewarding. However, they were sincerely persuaded by Wang, the Standing Committee member, County Magistrate Jin, Cai, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and District Chief Li, and they considered that if there were a fire and no one to rescue them due to their resignation, the local people would suffer a great loss. The comrades were unwilling to do so, so they maintained the spirit of serving the local community in the past, sacrificed everything, and reluctantly maintained their positions on the 3rd of this month. The case of Yao and Li will still proceed in accordance with legal procedures in order to achieve equality in both sentiment and law. The association stated that it was fortunate for the local area that the members took the overall situation into consideration, and it was feared that the citizens were not fully aware of this, so they issued this notice. All fire fighting equipment has been sent back by the County Party Department, the County Government, the District Public Office, and the County Chamber of Commerce.

Township Chief's Home Robbed 98

The home of Gao Zhongkui, the township chief of Datieqiao Township in the first district, located west of Changhai River, was suddenly visited by eleven bandits speaking local dialects and wearing blue and black short coats at about 11:00 last night. Six of them were on the lookout outside, and five of them broke into Township Chief Gao's house to rob. They stole five leather coats, more than one hundred cotton-padded and unlined clothes, a pair of gold rings, six yuan in cash, two briefcases, and six burlap sacks. After the robbery, which lasted until about 1:00 AM, they left the house and fled southwest. The bandits were armed with small knives and bayonets. The victim has reported the case to the First Branch Police Station, and Inspector Lu has sent Patrol Chief Wang Liansheng to investigate. A report has been submitted to the superiors for instructions to arrest the bandits.

Yu Jingtang, Director of the Suzhou Civil Affairs Department, Inspects Public Security Police 99

Yu Jingtang, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, held a spring inspection to understand the situation of the public security police on land and water in various counties. The ten counties of Wu, Kun, and Xi were designated as the first inspection area. Director Yu and his entourage arrived in Suzhou at 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd. Yesterday (the 3rd) at 8:00 AM, the county police officers and the police officers of the first water public security district gathered at Lao. Zhang Han, director of the Wu County Public Security Bureau, served as the commander-in-chief, and Zhu Aizhou and Yang Yuanpei, inspectors of civil police affairs, served as inspectors. Yu, Director of Civil Affairs, served as the reviewing officer. After the ceremony, the inspection began, including separate formations, formal training, cadre training, class training, platoon training, company training, unarmed exercises, martial arts, bayonet exercises, first aid exercises, rope arrest exercises, bicycle training, fire drills, and fire fighting techniques. It ended at about 11:00 AM. Then Yu, Director of Civil Affairs, gave a speech, and finally shouted slogans and closed the ceremony, and took pictures and dismissed. Yu, Director of Civil Affairs, is scheduled to go to Kunshan on the 4th, and then to Songjiang for inspection.

Wuxi: Armed Fight Injures People in Lujiang River 100

Lujiang River in the fourth district is an important passage to the lake. It is being dredged by Zhu, the district chief, who is responsible for the project. The entire river is divided into five sections, and about 3,800 villagers are working on the project. Since the start of construction on the 11th of last month, some parts have been completed, accounting for two-fifths of the total. The fourth class of the fourth Bao of Zhangshe Town is responsible for dredging the Niugang section. Yesterday, because the mud was difficult to walk on, they took several bundles of straw from Lujiang Village to use as foot rests, but without the consent of the villagers. A quarrel broke out with the women of the village. Then, the men and women of the village threw stones into the river. The villagers of Zhangshe Town could not bear it and an armed fight broke out. The security police rushed to the scene but could not stop it. They fired warning shots into the air before the crowd dispersed. At that time, more than 20 people were injured on both sides. In addition, a villager named Zou Jinhai, who was trying to mediate, was also beaten and his arm was broken. Afterwards, Jiang Shichu, the chief of the fourth Bao of Zhangshe Town, and Jiang Axi, the head of the fourth class, reported the situation to District Chief Zhu, who convened a meeting of both sides to persuade the villagers of Zhangshe Town to continue working. Each of the injured people on both sides would be given one yuan by the District Chief as medical expenses to quell the dispute.

Dredging of Zhenchang-Xixi Section of the Canal 101

Jiangsu Province is carrying out a disaster relief project, dredging the Zhenchang-Xixi Canal, and has allocated 1 million yuan in water conservancy bonds. The Zhenchang section has already started and is being carried out in stages. Tents have been set up along the canal for the workers to live in. The Wuxi section starts from Shouxing Wharf in the west of Wumu and ends at Shilulu Bridge in Luoshe Town, a total length of five kilometers (about nine li). Dams have also been built in stages to actively draw water. The dam of the Chen Gong Port tributary suddenly collapsed a few days ago. The Luoshe Supervision Office tried its best to block it, and it was finally closed that night, with only minor losses. The county government has ordered the district chiefs to recruit workers, stipulating that each Bao should send ten workers, with a daily wage of one jiao. Therefore, the villagers are very enthusiastic about working on the project.

Large Number of Yi-Li Refugees Given Money and Sent Back to Their Hometowns in Changzhou 102

Last year's drought caused the most damage to Yi and Li counties. This spring, refugees from the two counties, supporting the old and carrying the young, came to Changzhou to seek food. There are no less than several thousand people in the Ximen area. Local people, such as Lin Qiaobao, donated money to provide steamed buns and thin porridge to provide relief. Recently, as the spring plowing season is approaching, they raised a huge sum of several thousand yuan to help them return to their hometowns. At 8:00 AM on the 2nd, they hired 25 civilian ships, towed by three steamships. Mr. Lin and others personally escorted the ships. Before leaving, they took a group photo with the refugees as a souvenir and distributed rice flour, steamed buns, and other items. At about 6:00 PM, the refugees were all on board before the ships set sail. It is reported that every time they arrive at a place, each refugee will be given one yuan when they go ashore to help them make a living.

Haimen: Rice Merchants Continue Strike 103

The rice merchants here, in opposition to the Business Tax Bureau and the provincial inspectors' auditing and tax increases, have triggered a county-wide rice merchant strike. It has been two days and has yet to be resolved. The public has nowhere to buy rice and is very panicked. Barge crews, grain measurers, and sack loaders, all of whom rely on the daily activity of the rice market for their livelihood, have also become unemployed due to the rice market strike. On the morning of the second day, five to six hundred workers gathered and paraded through the bustling streets, going to the Party headquarters, the Business Tax Bureau, and the county government to petition for three demands: to immediately persuade the rice merchants to resume business so that livelihoods can be maintained; to abolish the investigation of accounts of various industries; and to dismiss the Finance Department committee member Liu, who caused this incident. Various departments responded separately. County Chief Zhai also addressed the crowds. In the afternoon of the second day, Party and government organizations held a discussion to resolve the issue. The solution decided was to convene a meeting with the rice industry leaders at 2:00 PM on the third day, urging them to resume business first. As for the tax reduction issue, the Chamber of Commerce Chairman Pang Jiegong and the Business Tax Bureau Chief Wu Zongbao were instructed to discuss solutions and submit them to the department for approval.

Haimen: Auction of Sino-British Pharmacy Property 104

The owner of the Sino-British Pharmacy in the county, Zhu Buping, was arrested by the Nantong District Commissioner's Office last autumn for selling narcotics, interrogated, and executed by firing squad. The house and goods were confiscated. Now, the Commissioner's Office has presented the matter to the provincial government, and with its approval, the store's property will be auctioned off for public funds according to the regulations for punishing narcotics offenders. Yesterday (the 31st), the county government was ordered to execute the order. After receiving the order, the county government decided to publicly auction the property on the 3rd of this month.

Wanted Bandit Huang Shourong Captured 105

Huang Shourong from Wangyang Village in the Sixth District has no fixed property and does not engage in legitimate work. He associates with bandits. In 1927, he colluded with others to kidnap Gong Yunsheng, a wealthy household in the district. Because the extortion was unsuccessful, Gong was killed and the body was destroyed to eliminate evidence. Gong's son, Gong Zuying, reported the case to the county government and offered a reward of five hundred yuan for his capture, but to no avail. In the spring of 1931, he led more than thirty bandits to rob the homes of Niu Zhuqiao, Fan Cunyi, and Sha Ruixiang, setting fire to more than ten houses. The victims reported to the county government, which sent officials to verify the facts and ordered a strict arrest. Huang, seeing that the situation was not good, hid in Shanghai. Now he has secretly returned home, plotting an uprising. Yesterday (the 31st), the county government learned of this, secretly instructed the Public Security Bureau to send police to arrest him. That night, Chen, the judge, opened a court to interrogate him and ordered him to be shackled and imprisoned.

Gu Tinghua's Son Kidnapped 106

Gu Tinghua, a farmer in Dongnan Erli Xu of Huifeng Township, is wealthy. His sixteen-year-old son, Guoxian, studies at Qixiu Middle School in Qilin Township. He asked for leave to return home the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, more than ten bandits speaking a Hakka dialect, wearing short clothes, and each holding a box gun, broke into the house that night. They rummaged through boxes and chests, searching thoroughly. Silver dollars, ornaments, and clothing worth about five hundred yuan were looted. Before leaving, they kidnapped Guoxian. Yesterday, the victim reported the incident to the county government for investigation.

Zhenjiang: Civil Affairs Department Issues Arrest Warrant for Fled Police Officer 107

Zhou Dingbo, a police officer at the Fourth Branch of the Taixian Public Security Bureau, was found to have extorted money when handling the voluntary surrender of Hu Lin and others. He was also bribed in the cases of Xie Zhongyin and Wen Han, both accused of being vagrants. He submitted a request for a month's leave to the county government but left his post and fled without approval. Director Yu of the Civil Affairs Department was extremely angry about this case. In addition to canceling the police officer's qualification as a graduate of the police academy and issuing an arrest warrant, he instructed the Taixian County Chief to supervise and strictly arrest him, and to investigate and detain the police officers who had fled with suspected corruption, to bring them to justice and punish them as a warning.

Dredging of River Beach Commences 108

The river beach along the river in this port has been gradually silted up over the years, causing inconvenience to transportation. After deliberation by the River Beach Dredging Committee, it was decided to dredge it in three sections. The first section, from the Customs House to the Xiaohuo Railway Station Wharf, is contracted by the Zhenjiang Municipal Construction Company and commenced on the 20th of last month. The Jinpu Railway Bureau believes that dredging this section of the river beach will greatly benefit railway freight and has specially lent more than a hundred mud transport vehicles to assist in the work. The second section, from Xiaohuo Railway Station to Nianyu Tao, and the third section, from Nianyu Tao to Longmenkou, are scheduled to begin in the winter.

Zhenjiang: Director Shen Inspects River Works in Dantu 109

Shen Baixian, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, traveled south yesterday by private car from the province to inspect the dredging projects of rivers in Jintan and other counties. He was accompanied by Secretary Qian Kaiying and Section Chief Hu from the First Section to Dantu. After arriving in Dantu, he went to the Dredging Canal Relief Office, inquiring in detail about the progress of all projects and the problems of mountain floods inundating farmland. He left Dantu by special express train to return to the province at about 5 PM.

Qingjiang: Counties Commemorate Martyr Tang 110

Tang Kezhi, captain of the Seventh Company of the Second Battalion of the Fourth Regiment of the Huai'an Provincial Security Team, stationed in Lianshui, was killed by bandits on the evening of the 4th of this month in Tianzhuang, Suyang County. Because the road was dark, he entered the bandits' lair alone and was killed. Afterwards, the county chiefs of Huai'an, Lianshui, and Shuyang, Yunlong, Shen Jinghua, Deng Xianghai, and Regiment Commander Jia Yunshan of this regiment, believed that Martyr Tang sacrificed for the public and should be commemorated. Therefore, a memorial service was held on the 31st at the Provincial Public Education Hall. More than a thousand representatives from various organizations and the public attended the service that day. Chairman Chen of Jiangsu Province and Director Xiang of the Security Office all sent elegiac couplets. The opening ceremony was held at 9 AM and the meeting adjourned at 1 PM.

Nantong: Provincial River Police Team Reorganized 111

The Jiangsu Provincial River Police Third District teams stationed in Nantong, Chongming, Hai'an, and Qidong counties were disarmed and reorganized into the Twelfth Team by Commissioner Zheng of the Nantong District, according to provincial orders. Wu Yanjie will train them in Nantong. More than two hundred officers and soldiers who were not selected for the team were paid their arrears in full on the 2nd and sent back to their hometowns with passports issued by the Commissioner's Office.

Xiang Zhizhuang Scheduled to Arrive in Nantong on the 10th 112

Xiang Zhizhuang, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office, is scheduled to arrive in Nantong on the 10th of this month to participate in the graduation ceremony of the Nantong District Security Team Platoon Leader Training Class and to inspect the team's training situation and the implementation of opium prohibition.

Pinghu: Over Ten Thousand Disaster Victims Flock to the City 113

Last year, there was a drought in the western regions of Haiyan, and more than three thousand refugees stayed in the eastern part of this county. The Charity Association and others provided rice porridge daily and sent them back to their hometowns half a month ago. Unexpectedly, there have recently been rumors that Pinghu will soon distribute grain seeds and that wealthy people from Shanghai have raised large sums of money to be distributed in the coming days. As a result, the refugees who had dispersed have regrouped inside and outside the city. Over seven thousand arrived the day before yesterday, and over three thousand arrived yesterday, with more arriving continuously. The area around Lugong Bridge in the eastern part of the city is filled with them. The Charity Association urgently cooked the remaining rice into thin porridge for temporary relief, but unfortunately, there was too little porridge and too many people to reach everyone. Today, the cake shop in front of the Great King Temple was looted by the disaster victims. A rural woman carrying dozens of dozens of foreign socks went to the factory to exchange them for money, but was pushed down and robbed. All the socks were taken in an instant. The county's task force and public security police went to suppress the situation and detained one disaster victim for interrogation.

Hangzhou: Designated Areas for Unified Management and Purchase of Cocoons 114

The Sericulture Control Committee of the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, considering that the spring silkworm season has already begun and the market is approaching, has divided the cocoon-producing counties and cities into ten major areas for unified management and purchase of spring cocoons. These include: Hangzhou City and Hang County; Yuhang, Lin'an, Yugan, and Changhua; Fuyang, Xindeng, Tonglu, and Fenshui; Zhuji, the southern part of Xiaoshan, and the western part of Shaoxing; Shangyu, Xinchang, Shengxian, and the eastern part of Shaoxing; Wukang, Anji, Changxing, and Xiaofeng; Xiaoshan, Shaoxing, and Nansha; Wuxing and Deqing; Jiaxing and Jiashan; Pinghu, Haiyan, Tongxiang, and Chongde. It is stipulated that all cocoons produced in the first to sixth districts will be purchased by the Committee under unified control. Cocoon merchants in the seventh to tenth districts must apply to the provincial and foreign silk factories for registration and approval, and the Committee will supervise and know their purchase activities. The measures have been approved and implemented by the provincial government yesterday.

Male and Female Teachers Commit Suicide 115

Hou Yunhan, a teacher at Chezhu Primary School in Chezhu Township, Changxing, and Qin Ruizheng, a female teacher at Lijia Lane Primary School outside the East Gate, fell in love and planned to marry. However, Qin's mother insisted on a bride price of four hundred yuan. Hou's income was meager and he could not afford it. On the 30th of last month, he borrowed money to go to the city and opened room 11 of the Datong Hotel. The two wrote several suicide notes, and both committed suicide with sickles. The scene was bloody and tragic. The case has been reported to the authorities, and the family has arranged for coffins and burial.

Ningbo: Robbery and Murder at Tiantong Temple 116

Tiantong Temple in Zhengdong is a famous temple in eastern Zhejiang with flourishing incense and offerings. The surrounding scenery is excellent, and tourists abound. Recently, a merchant from Shanghai and Ningbo, Wang Jinfu, brought his family to the temple to perform a Buddhist ceremony. The gold and jewels were dazzling, and the costumes were extravagant, which attracted the attention of bandits. The day before yesterday (the 31st), at around 5 PM, five bandits wearing blue and yellow long gowns entered the temple, carrying four box guns and one Browning rifle. They claimed to be there to perform Buddhist rituals and mingled with the worshippers. After dinner, they forcibly demanded money from the treasury. At that time, the abbot, Yuan Ying, was not in the temple. The receptionist monk, Benquan, resisted, which angered the bandits, who opened fire and shot him. He was hit in the chest and died on the spot. A worker, Changshouliang, was shot in the leg. After about an hour, the bandits looted more than a hundred silver dollars stored in the temple treasury, as well as eight gold and jewelry rings and more than three hundred yuan of paper money from Wang Jinfu's family, and fled through the back door. The next morning, the victim reported the case to the Fifth Public Security Sub-bureau for investigation.

—Reuters Commercial News Special Dispatch, April 3— 117

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 145 shillings, 7.5 pence, up 1 shilling, 6.5 pence.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The pound opened slightly lower, but rose before noon. The opening exchange rate for British-American was 4 dollars, 78 cents, 875, which was 1 cent, 875 lower than the closing price of British-American yesterday. It rose 75 in the first hour to 4 dollars, 79 cents, 625. At noon, it rose another 4375 to 4 dollars, 80 cents, 0625. The market was quite stable afterwards. Cotton and Wheat

British Wheat: The Chicago wheat market is still stable due to better sentiment and the international wheat market is also tight. There are signs of rain in the drought areas, but no rain has been seen yet. Opening prices rose slightly.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was stable at the opening. Trading was light before noon. At noon, the trading price for the July period was still 5 pence, 875, unchanged.

New York: The New York rubber market opened lower today, influenced by lower prices in London. The general trend among industry insiders is to wait for new developments.

Securities

New York: There is no special news today that can cause optimism for improved business. The unstable European political situation still makes people afraid to boldly operate. The domestic situation is also lackluster, so the securities market opened sluggishly and unevenly, with slight fluctuations in prices. Local News

Various Organizations Celebrate Children's Day Today 118

Party and Government Agencies to Convene at Moonlight Grand Theater; Children's Welfare Association and Others at Jiyang Bridge in Zhabei; Shanghai Radio Station to Broadcast Competition

Today, April 4th, is the fifth Children's Day in China. The Children's Welfare Association of the Municipal Party Department has initiated a celebration at the Moonlight Grand Theater on Bair Road, Ximen Road, today. The Municipal Government, Municipal Party Department, Education Bureau, Social Affairs Bureau, Health Bureau, and Children's Welfare Association will serve as the presidium. The Municipal Party Department has also sent a letter to the Education Bureau requesting each elementary school to send four representatives. The China Children's Welfare Association will also hold a Children's Day celebration today at Jiyang Bridge, Liuying Road, Zhabei. All schools will be closed for the holiday to celebrate Children's Day, and flags will be flown throughout the city.

Organizing Committee

The Children's Day Commemoration Committee includes Wu Tiecheng, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Cai Jingjun, Wu Kaixian, Tong Hangbai, Jiang Huaishu, Tao Baichuan, Lin Keting, Yang Hu, Yu Zuoting, Hu Shuyi, Zhu Xuefan, Chen Tiesheng, and Yu Zhenhui as the presidium. Zhang Hanyun will serve as the master of ceremonies, and Tong Muge and Du Mengsen will serve as recorders. Huang Xianggu, Huang E, Wu Xianren, Zhu Xiaochun, Bao Huizhong, Luo Gengyang, and Lin Yuxiang will be in charge of reception. Li Erbai, Cao Runsen, He Yuanming, Wu Di, Wang Guoping, Li Boqing, Qian Fugong, and Su Changjun will be in charge of security.

Celebrity Speeches

Cai Yuanpei, Wu Tiecheng, Ma Fengqi, Cai Zhoujun, Pan Gongzhan, Tang Guanyu, Lin Ketong, Huang Yanpei, Jiang Huaishu, Lu Jingshi, Wang Xiaoying, Liu Zhanen, Hu Shuyi, Wen Siying, and Wu Xingya have all been contacted and have agreed to spare time to give speeches on children's issues on the radio.

Entertainment Highlights

In addition to performances by Wanzhu, Xicheng, Feihong, Yangzheng, Xinmin, Danhua, Wuben, Shangwen, Tangwan, He'an, and Minglun Gaochang schools in the morning, there will also be educational films for children shown in the afternoon.
