Education News

Siamese Government Orders Compulsory Classes in Chinese Schools to Stop; Lin Tianduo Sends Letter to Siamese Ministry of Education Presenting New Ideas; Siamese Authorities Seem to Want to Find New Approaches 178

(Hua Lian News Agency, Bangkok) More than ten years ago, the Siamese government designated certain areas to implement compulsory education. Overseas Chinese in Siam also followed suit and stipulated certain areas as compulsory education zones. All children aged seven to fourteen were required to attend classes in compulsory schools. There has been no difference in the management since its establishment. Unexpectedly, on January 19th of this year, the Siamese Ministry of Education, citing the implementation of the constitutional ten-year education plan, notified all Chinese schools to uniformly stop compulsory classes from April 1st. Upon receiving this sudden notice, and learning that it was aimed specifically at Chinese schools, the Chinese schools wrote letters to the Prime Minister and the Minister of Education of Siam, requesting that they withdraw the order and allow the compulsory classes in Chinese schools to continue as before. It is recently heard that the Siamese Minister of Education seems to want to find another solution to the suspension of compulsory classes in Chinese schools. In early February, the Siamese Ministry of Education invited Lin Tianduo, the principal of Shantou Jiaoguang Middle School, to a meal to listen to his opinions. Later, Lin sent a letter to the Siamese Minister of Education at the end of February, offering a new method for continuing the compulsory classes in Chinese schools, in which he stated that the trial method would be of great benefit to Siam. His new method is as follows: (1) The proposed method is to enable Chinese schools to run education for education's sake, to assist the Siamese government, and there is no other purpose in it.

(2) The proposed method is to enable Chinese schools to not conflict with Siamese laws and government administration. Therefore, all Chinese schools within Siam that can abide by the national regulations and be incorporated into the correct track of rule, and can seriously run schools and assist the country in cultivating talents and seeking happiness for society, even if they are privately established, they will still be allowed to continue running.

(3) The new method is to exempt both the government and Chinese schools from economic losses. Because the compulsory classes in Siamese Chinese schools are closed, not only will more than one hundred Chinese schools immediately go bankrupt and thousands of teachers and staff will lose their jobs, but the government will increase the burden of more than 500,000 yuan of education funds every year, which will have a great adverse impact on the current financial situation of the Siamese country. Therefore, the compulsory classes in Chinese schools should still be maintained.

(4) The new method can win the obedience of overseas Chinese and the sympathy of the masses. Mutual The method is to enhance the cultural harmony and feelings between China and Siam.

(6) The proposed method is directly related to the occupation of overseas Chinese and indirectly related to the economy of the Siamese country. Therefore, its purpose is to meet the requirements of Siamese society and the country, to cultivate useful talents for overseas Chinese in Siam. For example, overseas Chinese in Siam mostly engage in industry and commerce and hold the center of the country's economy. However, in today's business world, it is impossible to apply if they do not know the Siamese Chinese English language. Therefore, this new method is to provide overseas Chinese with appropriate education, which is also beneficial to the development of overseas Chinese careers, and also has a good impact on the source of the Siamese national economy.

Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers College Education Research Association Holds Founding Meeting in the Province; Dozens of Research Proposals Submitted; Decision to Divide into Four Groups: Curriculum, Teachers, Etc.; Second Meeting Scheduled for the 20th of Next Month 179

(Zhenjiang News) In order to improve middle school teachers college education in Jiangsu Province, the Jiangsu Provincial authorities have decided, through deliberation by all middle schools in the province, to organize a Middle School Teachers College Education Research Association and hire domestic scholars and middle school principals as members. The association held its founding meeting yesterday (the 2nd) in the province, and held its first meeting, and dozens of research proposals were submitted. It was decided to divide into groups for discussion. The details are recorded below:

Attending Members

Liu Yiwei, Hu Huanyong, Hu Anding, Wang Guiying, Qiu Weiyu, Zhang Yi, Chen Lijiang, Hao Gengsheng (represented by Wu Bangwei), Wu Yunrui, These are education experts: Wu Yuandi, Zhou Houxu, Zheng Tonghe, Yan Liyang, Liu Hengjing, Jiang Xuezhu, Cao Chu, Zhou Yuxin, Sun Jiehuang, Xu Tao, Yu Yu, Huang Tongyi, Teng Songshi, These are middle school and teachers college principals, The representatives of the Department were Department Chief Zhou Fohai, Secretary Huang Shaohe, Section Chief Xue Zhongtai, etc.

Meeting Situation

The general meeting was held at 3 pm on the 2nd in the auditorium of the Education Department. The chairman was Zhou Fohai. After performing the formalities as usual, the report began. He briefly stated: "Today is the day of the founding meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers College Education Research Association. We are gathered here with experts to study and promote middle school teachers college education in Jiangsu Province. I hope all of you will use your past experience and research results to jointly research a thorough method and seek a dawn for the future of teachers college education in Jiangsu Province," and so on.

Important Resolutions

After the Department Chief finished the report, the discussion began. A. How to divide into groups for research (Decision) According to the nature of the various proposals, a total of four groups will be divided for research: (1) Curriculum Teaching Group, (2) Teacher Group, (3) Equipment and Funding Group, (4) Training and Military Management Group. The graduation examination proposal will be researched by the Curriculum Teaching Group. B. Can members be in two groups (Decision) Members can be in two groups. C. Will the group research be done by communication or meetings (Decision) Each group can consider the situation and use both communication and meeting methods. D. Date of the second general meeting (Decision) The date of the second general meeting is set for May 20th. The research reports of each group should be submitted in advance so that they can be submitted to the meeting for discussion.

Group Research

The chairman temporarily proposed: How should the list of members of each group be determined (Decision) (1) Curriculum Teaching Group, Zhou Xingbei, Cao Chu, Liu Yiwei, Hu Dingan, Dai Anbang, Qiu Weiyu, Hu Huanyong, Wu Yunrui, Wu Zixiu, Jiang Jingzhai, Huang Zhifu, Zhou Yigeng, etc. are 12 people, and Zhou Xingbei will convene. (2) Teacher Group, Zhou Yigeng, Zheng Xigu, Zhang Youliang, Chen Yimin, Hu Huanyong, Sun Jiehuang, Yu Yu, etc. are 7 people, convened by Zhou Yigeng (3) Equipment and Funding Group, Zheng Xigu, Xue Dong, Xu , Zhang Haicheng, Jiang Xuezhu, Wu Zixiu, Xi Songshi, etc. are 7 people, convened by Zheng Xigu. (4) Training and Military Management Group, Cao Chu, Zhang Haicheng, Liu Hengjing, Teng Shi, Wang Diancun, Zhou Xingbei, Yan Xiaofan, Sun Jiehuang, Huang Zhifu, etc. are 9 people, convened by Cao Chu. The staff of the Education Department can freely participate in the research of each group.

Overview of Proposals

After the meeting, each group held separate meetings to study the proposals. The proposers of the proposals this time included the Education Department, which raised research questions, including three questions on mathematics, Chinese, English, chemistry, and physics in terms of curriculum, and one question on graduation examinations. Member Xiang Shaoxuan raised two questions on curriculum and one question on teachers. There were three questions on the graduation examination. Members Sun Jiehuang and Zhou Yuxin raised one question on curriculum. Member Zheng Tonghe raised one research question on curriculum. Member Zhou Houxu raised 17 research questions on curriculum, Boy Scouts, military training, teacher training, teaching materials, and physical education funding. After detailed research by each group, they were summarized separately and specific plans were proposed.

Banquet for All

After the group research was completed, specific methods were proposed. At 6 pm, all members of the meeting were concentrated to study and exchange opinions with each other. The directors of each group reported the research results. The results were quite satisfactory, but they will not be announced until they are sorted out. At about 6 pm, in order to connect the feelings of all members, Department Chief Zhou specially hosted a banquet for all the members attending the meeting in the auditorium of the Education Department to celebrate. During the banquet, various issues of the Research Association were also studied. It was not until about 8 pm that everyone dispersed happily.

Ministry of Education Instructions to Two Universities: Transportation and Business Colleges - Order to National Chiao Tung University 180

(Nanking, 3rd) Based on the previous inspection report, the Ministry of Education issued an order to National Chiao Tung University on the 3rd, stating that the university's facilities are generally in order, the equipment is of a considerable scale, the faculty are dedicated to teaching, and the students are diligent and hardworking. The usual assessment of performance is quite strict, absenteeism is rare, the admission of new students is strictly managed, and both discipline and management are well regulated and earnestly implemented, which has created a good academic atmosphere. This is commendable and gratifying. However, the following points still need to be observed and improved to achieve perfection: 1. The organization and names of the university's colleges are mostly inconsistent with current education laws and regulations. According to Article 4 of the University Organization Law and Article 6 of the University Regulations, the College of Science should be renamed the College of Science, the College of Management should be renamed the College of Business, and the original departments should remain. The three colleges of Civil Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, and Electrical Engineering should be merged into the College of Engineering, with the three departments of Civil Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, and Electrical Engineering. Under the departments, groups may be established with the original names of (Sections) or (Divisions), which should be changed to (Departments) or (Groups) to comply with regulations. 2. The university's graduate school should follow the "Provisional Organization Regulations for University Graduate Schools" approved by the Ministry and promulgated by the Executive Yuan, and submit a detailed plan for approval by the Ministry. 3. The university has too many faculty members. Except for military training instructors, the names should be changed according to Article 13 of the University Organization Law. The number of lecturers and teaching assistants should be appropriately reduced, and a dedicated professor system should be strictly implemented. 4. The number of university staff, service personnel, and security guards is excessively large and should be reduced. Special expenses should be tightened to use the savings to supplement equipment. 5. Many lower-level courses in the university are taught purely in English, which may hinder the progress of students' studies. The weekly teaching hours in each college are more than 30 hours, leaving little opportunity for extracurricular study. These issues must be corrected. 6. The university's upper campus and library are old and decaying and may collapse at any time. Efforts should be made to rebuild them. The equipment in the colleges of engineering should be strengthened to facilitate teaching. You are hereby ordered to comply and report.

Order to National Shanghai College of Commerce

The order to National Shanghai College of Commerce roughly stated that most of the faculty members of the college are dedicated to their duties and are diligent. Disciplinary management and various examinations can be implemented seriously. The students are simple and diligent, abide by the school rules, and the absence of absenteeism is decreasing. The academic atmosphere has gradually become better, which is commendable and gratifying. However, the following points still need to be observed and improved: (1) In addition to handling other cases for the college's construction of school buildings, completion should be sought as soon as possible. (2) The college's office expenses account for more than 28%, while the purchase fee is only 900 yuan, less than 1%. The allocation is inappropriate. The college's books have been lost after the war and the existing collection is insufficient for application. Efforts should be made to reduce office expenses and add them gradually. (3) The college's part-time teachers should be reduced, and the teaching time of full-time professors should be reduced if it is too short. Modifications should be made as appropriate. (4) The college's course materials for each subject should focus on domestic practical problems to enhance teaching effectiveness. You are hereby ordered to comply with the improvement report.

Ministry of Education: Medical Education Committee Meeting Today to Finalize the Medical Curriculum 182

The Ministry of Education's Medical Education Committee held a meeting last year to elect members to draft the medical curriculum for university medical schools and other institutions. After drafting the draft, the entire committee revised and supplemented it, and the members then divided the work to revise and organize it again. After the members were assigned to their respective tasks, they successively sent the revised curriculum standards to the Ministry. They are now complete. The Ministry of Education has scheduled a committee meeting at the Ministry at 8:00 a.m. today (the 4th) to gather experts and committee members to discuss the draft curriculum standards for university medical schools and specialist medical schools and to make the final decision. After this curriculum is developed, the curriculum standards for other colleges in the university will be drawn up. Furthermore, this curriculum standard plan will be more specific from the outline. The standard, which was once formulated a few years ago with many complex details, has reduced the obstacles to consistent implementation and the difficulty of uneven levels in future examinations.

Wang Teh-chien Invents New Character Indexing Method 188

Mr. Wang Teh-chien is employed at the Municipal Zhenru Primary School. He enjoys studying the six scripts in his spare time and is particularly skilled at iron pen calligraphy. Recently, he has developed a new character indexing method based on his previous work. He divides characters into categories based on their shape and uses strokes to create numbers. His mnemonic is "nine character shapes, eight mother strokes, three outlines and four categories." The character indexing method is indeed more convenient than any other method. He is currently editing a dictionary.

University Teachers' Association Promotes Adult Practical Education - Yesterday Specially Issued a Declaration on Adult Remedial Education - Decided to Conduct Jointly with the Cultural Construction Association 194

The Shanghai University Teachers' Association held its 18th Standing Committee meeting at its meeting place on Avenue Foch yesterday at 5:00 p.m. Huang Hsien-chang, Chiang Chen-san, Chen Kao-yung, Chiang Tzu-pai, and others attended. Chen Kao-yung chaired the meeting, and Yu Ta-san recorded the minutes. The discussion focused on the issue of adult remedial education as follows:

Promoting Adult Practical Education

The agenda was as follows:

(1) How to promote adult remedial education. It was resolved that: A. A declaration would be issued; B. The scope of education would be Shanghai; C. The target audience would focus on adult men and women's literacy education; D. The main body of education would be the Association in conjunction with the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association, as well as various organs and groups in the special zone and individuals enthusiastic about adult remedial education; E. Implementation method: It was decided to jointly convene the Shanghai Special Zone Adult Remedial Education Promotion Association with the Shanghai Branch of the Cultural Construction Association to conduct jointly. (2) The agenda for the five joint meetings of the Executive Committee and the Supervisory Committee was decided to be held on April 21st at 2:00 p.m. at the Chung She on Weihaiwei Road. (3) Supplementary election of lecturers for academic lectures: It was decided to elect Lin Chung-ko, Chiang Chien-pai, Kang Hsuan-yi, and Chen Kao-yung to serve in this role. (4) How to promote membership surveys: It was decided to be handled by the Document Section. (5) It was decided to hold a standing committee meeting at 1:00 p.m. on April 21st. The meeting adjourned after the agenda was completed.

Issuing a Declaration on Integrating Knowledge and Action

The Shanghai University Teachers' Association's Declaration on Promoting Adult Remedial Education is as follows: To all cultural and educational institutions and teachers and students of schools across the country: We believe that the fundamental reason for China's weakness and decline is the invasion of international imperialism, but the low level of national culture and the weakness of national consciousness are also major reasons. Examining the educational situation of the major powers, they are far superior to China. More than 90% of the people in Germany, France, England, the United States, and Japan have received national compulsory education. Even in the Soviet Union, before the war, compulsory education accounted for only 50% of the total population. After the revolution, it vigorously carried out the literacy campaign and promoted basic education, which has now increased to 96%. It can unite and defend the country. Looking back at China, only 20% of the people receive compulsory education. Out-of-school children and adult illiterates are rampant in cities and villages. Basic knowledge of personal life is still lacking. How can they know the responsibility of the nation and the rise and fall of the country? The Association believes that the compulsory implementation of national compulsory education is a fundamental solution, which requires our government to raise funds and plan comprehensively. However, the most important short-term solution is for the national intellectuals to vigorously carry out adult remedial education and completely eliminate illiteracy. The foundation of national cultural construction and the path to national self-reliance lie in this. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau advocated literacy education and planned to implement it in Shanghai first. It is indeed a cultural movement that sees the key to the problem and is in line with the national conditions. We hope that the national cultural and educational institutions, groups, and teachers and students of major and secondary schools will do their best to open adult remedial classes, combining literacy education with civic education, so that all people in the country can read and know the nation and protect the race. To know but not to act is the shame of the wise. To have people but not to teach them is the humiliation of the scholars. May our national intellectuals sweep away the past habit of idle talk, rise up and create a style of clear discernment and resolute action, strive to eliminate illiteracy, and revitalize the Chinese nation. The members of this Association will naturally integrate knowledge and action and encourage each other with people across the country.

Publication of "China Review" 196

In recent years, new magazines have emerged like bamboo shoots after rain, forming a rare scene in our country's history. However, there are still few that make practical research, criticism, and contributions to various aspects of politics and society. Scholars Lei Chen, Hsu Yi-chiao, and Luo Hong-chao in Peking and Shanghai, in view of this, have specially organized the China Review Society (the address is at No. 21 Hongwu Street, Nanking) to focus on national revitalization, research the problems of revitalization in politics, economics, education, diplomacy, finance, and society, and plan to publish one issue of "China Review" per month for systematic publication and introduction. The inaugural issue of the publication was published on April 1, and includes "Is China Not Suitable for Dictatorship?" by Hsu Yi-chiao, "Cultivating the Spirit of a Fighter to Build a New China" by Lei Chen, "Dictatorship and China" by Li Chien-hua, "Improvement of Sino-Japanese Relations" by Luo Hong-chao, "The Conflict Between Britain and Japan and the Problem of Anglo-American Cooperation" by Tsai Ke-cheng, "The Shackles of Economic Development in Rural China" by Hu Ming-lung, and "The Basic Problems of National Revival" by Hsu Sung-chou, all of which have unique perspectives. Other research papers and narrations are all the result of careful consideration. In addition, the inaugural issue of the publication is intended to be widely distributed to domestic cultural institutions for criticism, and the intended pricing for Sheng Ching will be lowered to make it easier for readers to purchase.

Assault on Referee Case: Three Tung Wah Players Disqualified; Wan Sheung-wah, Chan Ka-kui, and Luk Chung-yan Severely Punished; Result of the Day Stands, Westerners Beat Tung Wah 3-2 199

Last Saturday, during the Western League A Division match between Tung Wah and the Westerners at the Shanghai Recreation Ground, Tung Wah players assaulted referee Baine during the second half with fifteen minutes remaining, causing a great uproar. According to the resolution of the Western League Football Association Executive Committee, three players, including Wan Sheung-wah, have been disqualified from participating in matches, and the result of the match stands, with the Westerners winning 3-2. The details are as follows:

Resolution of the Case

The Western League Executive Committee, in order to uphold the spirit of sportsmanship and respect the authority of referees, resolved (1) to suspend Wan Sheung-wah, who assaulted the referee, from competition for the remainder of this season and the entire 1935-1936 season; (2) Chan Ka-kui and Luk Chung-yan, for their poor behavior, are suspended from competition for the remainder of this year, until December 31, 1935, and may only be allowed to participate in matches from January 1, 1936; (3) the result of the day stands, with the Westerners defeating Tung Wah 3-2.

Tung Wah Meeting

The Tung Wah Football Club, after receiving notification of the Western League's decision to punish, has specifically scheduled an emergency meeting of all players from both the A and B teams for 7:00 PM today at the club's headquarters at 11 Route Joffre, where they will make a statement. All are requested to attend on time.

This Week's Schedule

This week's schedule includes only one match, on Saturday at 3:00 PM, between Tung Wah and the Western Merchants in the A Division, at the Recreation Ground, with referee Ah Kuk-sang, and linesmen Kingsley and David.

E Division Final

Furthermore, the E Division League has concluded, with St. Francis and Starlight scoring the same number of points and tied for first place. A final match must be held to determine the championship, scheduled for 10:00 AM on the 14th of this month. The location will be announced later.

Grand Farewell to the Liang Chiang Southern Tour Team in the Philippines 204

The Liang Chiang basketball team, since its southern expedition, has been gone for nearly two months. It first arrived in the Philippines, and news of its victories has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the team has left the Philippines for Surabaya, and must pass through Batavia, Singapore, Saigon, Hong Kong, and other places before returning to Shanghai. The grand occasions of its arrival and departure in the Philippines are briefly recorded below:

War Record in the Philippines This time, the Philippine Chinese Athletic Association organized the All-Philippines Women's Basketball Championship, held during the Carnival. Participants included the American Central Team, the Philippine All-Stars, the All-Philippines Combined Team, the Chun Hui Team from Amoy, and Liang Chiang, for a total of five teams (using a double round-robin system). Liang Chiang was able to overcome all of them, winning the championship, and earning praise from people of various countries traveling in the Philippines. The Chinese community regarded it as unparalleled glory. Each game had thousands of spectators, and the Li spiking field of the previous Far East Games was filled to capacity, a truly unprecedented scene.

Record of Celebration Banquets After the Liang Chiang team arrived in the Philippines, various sectors hosted banquets one after another, including the Chinese Consulate General in the Philippines, the Chinese Association, the General Branch of the Chinese Kuomintang, the Shang Yi Society, the Chung Hsi School, Western sports organizations, Western women's basketball teams, the Ching Nan Athletic Association, the President of Philippine Women's University, the General Chamber of Commerce, the Taiyuan Hall, various Chinese merchants, and many banquets from foreign residents in the Philippines, enhancing mutual feelings.

Surabaya Cables Welcome Liang Chiang stayed in the Philippines for a total of three weeks, which was quite long. Because they repeatedly won victories, Surabaya had already heard the news and sent cables of welcome. The team then boarded the Cizinecara on the 7th to leave the Philippines. The Consul General and his wife, the Athletic Association, and various groups all came to the port to see them off, shaking hands and saying goodbye, waving ribbons and handkerchiefs, making the hosts and guests feel sad.

Before the Development of the New Cotton Policy, American Cotton Sellers Feel Uneasy 215

Yesterday, American cotton opened higher due to good news from Liverpool. Dealers bought in, and spot prices were firm. Spot traders bought near-term months, so near-term prices rose by 9 to 11 points. Far-term months also rose by 3 to 4 points. Subsequently, because the government's new cotton policy had not yet been developed, the market felt uneasy. Dealers in New Orleans and locally sold, and bullish investors closed out positions, so prices gradually declined. When prices fell, dealers continued to buy, and short-sellers covered their positions slightly. According to estimates from the New Orleans Cotton Exchange, as of the end of March, a total of 2,277,000 tons of fertilizer had been used. It is estimated that spot prices fell by 5 points, and futures prices fell by 3 to 13 points. British cotton spot prices rose by 2 points, and futures prices rose by 5 to 7 points. Indian cotton rose because short positions were covered. Deliveries were not high. Speculators bought White Rose Creek May futures and were firm. Silk and Tea: The Crisis of Waxed Zhenmei – Tea Merchants Should Change Their Methods 221

The green tea from the northwest and west roads of Wuyuan has always been known for its workmanship. The Zhenmei tea they produce uses various coloring materials such as beeswax, indigo, and talc. The color is quite beautiful and has been sold to Africa and Aaron . . . for a long time. However, since . . . this waxed tea has been greatly affected. Recently, Aaron has also increased import taxes on Chinese tea, and there are rumors that Africa will ban the import of waxed tea. Judging from the above situation, Wuyuan green tea should change its production method and prohibit coloring. Then, Morocco and the United States can sell it like Tunxi tea.

Shanghai City Special Edition for Celebrating Children's Day

Children's Sports and the Future of the Nation 226

— Wu Tiecheng

Ancient Chinese governance combined education and nurturing, emphasizing raising the young and caring for the elderly. It is because children possess innate intelligence, pure hearts, and lively natures. Their intellect, virtue, and physical well-being are all superior to those of adults. If we can educate and nurture them properly, each according to their abilities, it will be easy to cultivate them into talents for society and improve the quality of the nation.

In modern times, all countries undergoing political reforms pay great attention to the protection of people's lives. They even provide constitutional guarantees for children's lives and rights. The new German constitution after the war is a clear example. Article 122 of the German constitution stipulates: "Overwork of children, as well as moral, mental, and physical neglect, shall be protected. The federal government and other public bodies shall take the necessary measures for this." Articles 92 and 120 also contain provisions on family health and compulsory education. Labor laws in various countries are even more detailed in protecting children, with strict and special restrictions and care in laws regarding working age, working hours, education level, and physical health.

Our country's sages did not neglect the issue of children. They said, "Men have their duties, women have their homes, the strong have their work, and the widowed, orphaned, lonely, disabled are all cared for." It is also said: "Respect the old of your family, and extend that respect to the old of others; love the young of your family, and extend that love to the young of others." Their spirit of caring for and paying attention to children is clear. Unfortunately, in recent times, education has been abandoned. Not only the state and society neglect children, but even parents and teachers do not know their responsibilities for education. They spend their days together talking about meaningless things, engaging in licentious behavior, and ruining their minds and bodies. Children are the future spirit of the nation and the cornerstone of the country. If we continue to ignore them, the harm it will inflict on the nation is unimaginable.

Today, on the anniversary of Children's Day, I received a draft request, so I took the time to express my feelings. I sincerely hope that those engaged in children's sports today will pay close attention to and study children's lives, children's health, children's welfare, etc., so that countless lively, pure, and intelligent children will not be corrupted by bad environments, but will grow into talents for the country and society. The benefits to the nation's future will be immeasurable.

Nurturing Uprightness from Childhood: Special Publication for Children's Day 227

— Inscribed by Wang Zhaoming

New Children's Life and Social Transformation 228

— Wu Xingya

Lao Tzu said: "Changing customs and habits starts gradually." Social customs are the basis for establishing a country's destiny. The formation of customs comes from gradual influence, so their removal is not the work of a day or two. The basis of social transformation lies in transforming the lives of the people. If the lifestyle is appropriate, then physiologically and psychologically, they will unconsciously move towards norms, and a good society will be formed!

According to the results of learning psychology experiments, human activities, apart from their instincts, can be expressed in various social actions due to the effect of habit. Once a habit is formed, if it is good, it will be enjoyed for life, and if it is bad, it will be difficult to correct. Therefore, when it comes to changing customs and habits, we must pay attention to the cultivation of habits. Since adults' habits are not easy to change, then the childhood life, education, and cultivation of various habits that adapt to society while improving society should be our major mission!

Now, children are affected by bad social habits, and everywhere they show the bad habits of seeking ease, taking shortcuts, being decadent, passive, scattered, and selfish. The failure of the new education in recent decades is also the reason for social unrest. From now on, we should put effort into children's education to instill in them beliefs in creation, service, struggle, and labor, as well as the spirit of loyalty, diligence, righteousness, and chivalry. These beliefs and spirits should be gradually trained in daily life, cultivated into habits, and guarded without loss. Today's children are the adults of the future. If we pay attention to social transformation, we cannot but base it on all aspects of children's lives in their flourishing years.

New Life Movement and Children's Health 229

— Li Tingan

Does life have new and old? Both are me. Yesterday's me, viewed today, is the old life. Tomorrow's me, viewed today, is the new life. Is it that life has new and old? Today's yesterday is like the day before yesterday's tomorrow. Will today's tomorrow not be the yesterday of the day after tomorrow? What is called life is like the opening and fading of flowers, the waxing and waning of the moon. That which passes is like that, and that which comes is like this. How can there be a distinction between new and old? I have heard that those sages who cultivate themselves say, "If I hear the Way in the morning, I can die in the evening." How eager they are for a new life! However, they say, "If I were given a few years, I would be able to learn the Book of Changes and avoid great mistakes." Their consistent life seems to have new and old, but in reality, there is no distinction between new and old. How easy it is to connect, and how difficult it is to achieve! Life has no categories, but life has progress and stagnation. Advancing is new, and stagnating is old. Therefore, there can be eternal renewal, and there can be abandonment of the old today. Alas, is life new? It is not new; it is simply expanding and enriching what already exists. Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek promoted the New Life Movement in Nanchang, scrupulously emphasizing propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. He calls it new in name, but seeks its meaning in the ancients. Is he perhaps seeking the way of the gentleman who devotes himself to the fundamentals? Children's health is an old term, but it is also the New Life. . . . Those who publicize it in newspapers and broadcast it far and wide, why not call it an old term? Although those who often speak empty words, today put them into practice. Those who often despise, today follow them. Those who often use it as a banner, today put it into practice physically. Why not call it a New Life? Alas, in the warm spring, only the grass and trees gain new meaning. Moreover, in this New Life Movement, we are looking forward to our comrades working for the happiness of children. Why not rise up? My comrades, let us encourage ourselves.

People at Birth Are Naturally Good; Natures Are Similar, Habits Differ 230

— Ye Chucang's inscription for Children's Day

Creating Happiness for Children 231

— Inscribed by Kong Xiangxi

Overview of the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee 232

(1) Purpose: This committee aims to promote social awareness of children's status and develop children's welfare, striving for the happiness of all children in the city.

(2) Historical Outline: In March of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), various sectors of Shanghai jointly organized the Preparatory Committee for the Shanghai Municipal Celebration of Children's Day. At that time, administrators from the four bureaus of Public Security, Social Affairs, Education, and Health, along with enthusiastic social workers, recognizing the importance of the children's movement and feeling that the development of children's welfare in the city required a permanent governing body responsible for implementation to be effective, proposed during the second preparatory meeting that Preparatory Committee members Pan Gongzhan, Hu Shuyi, and others formally organize the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee as the main body in Shanghai to lead children's welfare and promote children's happiness. Hu Shuyi was appointed to draft the organizational regulations for the Children's Welfare Committee, which were submitted and passed by the preparatory committee. Subsequently, in May, the directors of the four bureaus of Public Security, Social Affairs, Education, and Health submitted a request to the municipal government for approval and registration, and requested the mayor to serve as the president. In June, President Wu Tiecheng convened the inaugural meeting at the municipal government, immediately electing executive committee members. The individuals elected were Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Chen Heqin, Hu Shuyi, and Liu Wang Liming. The organizations elected were the China Child Welfare Association representative Wang Guanyi and the Children's Morning Post representative Zhao Zengqi, among others. Subsequently, recognizing the difficulties faced by working-class laborers in factories regarding childcare, the committee established a separate Nursery Business Committee to prepare for the establishment of nurseries. In August, in accordance with regulations, groups and experts in the city enthusiastic about children's welfare were invited to serve as members of the committee, working together to advance the nursery business. The first nursery was established in Nanshi as a pilot. On September 20th of the same year, during the committee's first executive committee meeting, Hu Shuyi proposed that the government designate a "Children's Year" to promote and advance children's welfare. The China Child Welfare Association was also requested to submit a request to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for forwarding to the central government for approval. The committee requested the mayor to appoint Yu Hongjun and 183 others as members of the Children's Year Committee. This was the origin of last year's Children's Day in the city and this year's nationally designated Children's Year, and is also one of the committee's important undertakings.

(3) Departmental Operations:

(1) Children's Protection Department: Upholds children's rights, investigates and provides relief in cases of child abuse, child trafficking, or other infringements of children's rights, and works to liberate children who have been harmed.

(2) Children's Health Department: Guides society to pay attention to children's health, conducts children's health competitions, investigates the living conditions of child laborers in factories and businesses, and makes improvements as needed.

(3) Children's Research Department: Tests children's physiology and psychology, examines children's character, intelligence, and physical strength, and researches new methods for nurturing and educating children.

(4) Children's Enterprise Department: Promotes and invents various new businesses beneficial to children's lives, such as the production of various items related to clothing, food, housing, transportation, entertainment, and culture, or the publication of periodicals, etc.

(4) Affiliated Enterprises:

(1) Labor Nursery: Located near Panfang on Penglai Road, it specializes in caring for the children of laborers, thereby reducing the burden on working women and increasing their productivity. Initially, it only offered daytime care, but starting this month, due to its proven effectiveness, it has also begun offering nighttime care.

(2) Children's Library: There are two locations, one in the Municipal He'an Elementary School on North Chengdu Road on Xinzha Road, and one near Panfang on Penglai Road. Due to financial constraints, the committee co-operates with the Children's Morning Post.

(3) Children's Cinema: There is no fixed location. During holidays, screenings are held in the Hunan and Zhabei districts. The Hunan district screenings are at the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road, and the Zhabei district screenings are at the He'an Elementary School on North Chengdu Road on Xinzha Road. Recently, it has partnered with the Moonlight Grand Theater, designating Tuesdays, Thursdays, and Fridays as Children's Film Days, exclusively screening educational films for children at discounted rates.

(5) Funding: The committee's funding is divided into regular expenses and business expenses. Regular expenses are requested from the municipal government, while business expenses are raised by the committee as needed.

(6) Address: The committee's address is near Panfang on Penglai Road in Nanshi. For the convenience of all sectors, a liaison office is also located in the city center at the Municipal Education Bureau and at the Children's Morning Post at 205 Shandong Road.

Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee's Message to Children Nationwide for the 5th Children's Day 233

Dear children nationwide:

Today should be your happiest day because the 5th Children's Day has arrived!

The meaning of Children's Day can be explained in two ways. On the one hand, because we Chinese have traditionally not paid attention to children's well-being, Children's Day is meant to promote it. On the other hand, because our Chinese children have traditionally not known the importance of their own position, Children's Day is meant to encourage them to become aware.

Adults not promoting children's well-being is certainly unfair to children. Children not knowing the importance of their own position is unfair to themselves! You must know: you are the treasures of the nation. The future of the nation will depend on you to support and maintain it. If you do not know the importance of your position and do not strive to fulfill your responsibilities, you will not only be unfair to yourselves but also to the nation.

Children, we already know the importance of your position and recognize you as the treasures of the nation. Therefore, from now on, we will strive to promote children's well-being. You, too, should know the importance of your position and strive to fulfill your responsibilities.

Children, come, you work hard for yourselves, and we will work hard for you. Let us work together!

Fishing 236

— Weijing

Dropping a line is not considered vulgar in China. The most famous story in history, passed down for thousands of years and still popular, is the story of Jiang Taigong fishing. Secondly, there is Yan Ziling's Fishing Terrace in western Zhejiang, which makes people linger and admire. As for the famous song "Old Fisherman," countless people have recited and sung it. Although the position of that famous song has been taken away by modern dance troupes, "Old Fisherman" is no longer commonly on people's lips, but its sad and stirring melody can still be heard from time to time in the streets and alleys.

Indeed, in ancient China, some people resigned from their official positions and retired to the countryside, holding a wine cup in their left hand and a fishing rod in their right, seeking poetic inspiration in the vast expanse of misty waters. Others were unsuccessful in the literary field or stumbled in their careers, with a belly full of depression and complaints, with nowhere to vent, so they found a stream or corner, dropped a fishing rod, spent their years, and used it to forget their sorrows and hatreds. Therefore, in the water paintings of artists, adding an old fisherman returning from fishing or currently fishing can enhance the poetry and liveliness of the painting.

However, just as oranges change when transplanted north of the Huai River, fishing is the same. Because dropping a line is a refined and profound pastime in China, but in foreign countries, it has become an espionage activity to explore the depth of harbors and the speed of currents.

The former is to embellish the lakes and mountains, how tranquil, the latter is preparing to shed blood, full of murderous intent. Both are fishing, but their natures are so different, where does one even begin?

Spring Cold 237

— Huoxueming

Everyone sings the praises of spring's arrival. The clouds in the sky are so light, the water in the river is so gentle, the peach blossoms smile, the willows dance, and even the women on the streets have shed their black furry fur coats and changed into thin new shirts, probing the new coolness that the east wind brings. Needless to say, the yellow dust on Longhua Road has been stirred up by the light hooves of horses, and the fragrant charm of peach groves everywhere has been released for poetry-seeking companions, while the pens of writers easily slip out the clichéd phrase "Spring has arrived" on the manuscript paper.

But spring is also like a beautiful girl, her eyebrows smiling, her eyes speaking, her lips revealing charm, her arms writing spring love; but sometimes she will also restrain her lively posture and make a serious appearance. Therefore, people look forward to a sunny and warm spring, but because of a snow, a rain, or a night of wind, they repeatedly return to the bitter cold of late winter. The sad fate of those flowers and leaves that cannot withstand the cold and freeze, withering and falling to the ground in the blink of an eye, cannot be avoided after all. Look! Aren't the daughters all rummaging through the bottom of their boxes for the heavy furs and thick coats they just put away?

When you think warmth belongs to you, you must look back to see the cold creeping behind you, waiting for an opportunity to strike!

The companions enjoying the spring are going from the city to various mountains and rivers to seek spiritual nourishment. Everyone is injecting rich joy into their smiles, but in the weather of light clouds and soft sunlight, a dove's call at dusk must warn you that tomorrow morning, when you wake up from your pillow, you will be disappointed by the sound of rain.

Do not dislike the heavy and clumsy winter fur coats, do not indulge in only wearing newly made spring shirts; occasional coldness will tell you a kind of life philosophy beyond travel knowledge!

Put on the Last Supplement 238

— Yue

Little Western Paradise 239

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eleven: Evening Talk of a Miserable Life, Originally a Dream; Scattered Footprints, Wind and Rain Too Deceitful

Based on what he said today, he should not have a smile on his face with the kind of life he leads. Even if he smiles at people, it's not really a smile, but a cry. Who in society can see that someone else's smile is a cry? So, a person who smiles while crying can only smile while crying for the rest of their life. This evening, the lamp was dim, the house was dark, and the wind blew the door. I don't know if Yang and Jia were crying or laughing. However, the next day, Yang Huanhua had three dollars in his pocket, which gave him a little comfort. In the metropolis of Xi'an, you can still see the hard-working spirit of the northwestern people, as citizens get up as soon as it dawns. If someone is still not up after eight o'clock after spring, there must be something wrong with them. That day, Yang Huanhua woke up at nine o'clock. The half-closed door was blown wide open by the wind, and it was cool and drafty, even the sleeping curtains were fluttering a bit. Huanhua immediately stuck his head out and looked outside, only to see that the sky outside the window was gloomy. It seemed that the sun had not yet emerged from the earth. Huanhua thought that he seemed to have slept very soundly and should have had a longer time, so why hadn't the sun come out yet? Just as he was concentrating, his throat was choked by the cold wind, and he couldn't help coughing twice in a row. The waiter stuck his head in and looked around at the door, then gently called out, "Miss Yang, it's time to get up, it's already past nine o'clock." Huanhua said, "Oh! It's past nine o'clock. Is it raining?" The waiter said, "Slanting wind and fine rain, it was noisy all night yesterday, didn't you know?" Huanhua put on his clothes while laughing, "I really didn't feel anything. Has Mr. Jia in the next room gotten up?" The waiter said with a smile, "He's sleeping soundly just like you." Huanhua immediately put on his clothes and called the waiter to bring tea and water in. The waiter kept going in and out, always smiling at him. (173)

Records of the Fragrant Imperial Aroma 240

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

I can say that it is extremely difficult for anything small or inconspicuous to escape the Empress Dowager's eyes. So, I feel that every time I accompany the Empress Dowager on a stroll in the Summer Palace, I can always get many new insights, because as we walk along, she only needs to take a casual look and can immediately see many inappropriate arrangements or missing pieces that should be added. After she points them out, these inappropriate arrangements or omissions must be immediately removed or supplemented; otherwise, the person responsible for management will be in great trouble.

Ah! Just imagine how beautiful and lovely a stone floor filled with hundreds of interwoven deep red and light green colored silk threads must be! Moreover, they are arranged very neatly, a row of red, a row of yellow, a row of blue; looking at them from afar, they are really like a rainbow in the sky. The girls walk back and forth in these rainbows. They dare not leave for a moment; because these silks often need people to turn them over, to avoid too much or too little exposure to the light. If they are not dried well, they cannot be used, and the many efforts previously spent on reeling, washing, brushing, and dyeing are wasted. However, it is not easy for us laymen to distinguish whether the results after drying are good or bad. Apart from these little girls who specialize in silk production, only our intelligent and versatile Empress Dowager has this extraordinary eyesight. (284)

Yu San 241

— Baozhi

Yu San, a man who has experienced many setbacks and suffered major stimuli, is released from prison and wants to change his life and struggle again, but when he returns to his former residence, his wife and children are scattered, and the scenery is completely different. Therefore, he has to wander, searching for his flesh and blood and lover in the vast sea of dust.

In order to seek a stable life, he accidentally runs into a former friend, who recommends him to work as a messenger in the vault of a bank. Little does he know that the person in charge of the vault is his own son.

Later, as time goes by, he slowly confirms his suspicions and understands everything. His old friend from twenty years ago has occupied his beloved wife, made a fortune, and become the manager of this bank. His son is the director of the vault. However, he has already changed his life. He doesn't expose it and continues to live his life as a servant.

One day, the director of the vault escorts funds to another port and is plotted against by a group of bandits who use women as bait. Yu San bravely fights to take the funds back from the bandits, but he is shot and killed by the arresting officers.

This is a story from the new film "Human Relations" produced by Mingxing, which has the style of the Western film "The Fugitive." The portrayal of "paternal love" in the film is truly able to fully express its essence. In the near future, the film will be released at the Xinguang Theater in this city. Viewers who like the rough-line style are worth seeing it.

You Shao Returns 243

— Sun Choucheng

The scenery of Yue is the most beautiful in the southeast. This time, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, and Pei Yunqing initiated a spring tour group, inviting close friends from all walks of life in Shanghai and Hangzhou to visit Shao. On the morning of the 26th, they crossed the river, and on the afternoon of the 27th, they returned to Hangzhou. Although the trip was only two days, they saw many famous places. On the Shanyin Road, they were overwhelmed with attractions. The situation of this tour is briefly recorded as follows:

Upon arrival in Shao, because the Shaoxing branch of the Silk Industry Bank opened that day, more than a hundred people went to congratulate them, eating the Guan Sheng Yuan refreshments they had prepared until the bottom of the basins were facing the sky. At eleven o'clock, they took a car to Donghu, where small boats were prepared. They floated on the lake, passing through the Xiantao Tao Gong Cave, looking up at the high rocks, some facing each other like doors, and some standing alone upside down. The water was deep blue, as if sitting in a well. After feasting at Shuiyue Pavilion, they took a car to Fanjia Village Station, and then took a boat to Houshan. The scenery along the way was excellent. Artists such as Huang Binhong, Xie Gongzhan, and Wang Jiyuan drew sketches everywhere, obtaining a rich harvest. At the Yanluo Cave, they tasted tea in the newly built Fuyan Villa of Mr. Wang Xiaolai, facing the mountain and facing the water, which was extremely elegant. Beside it was a cloud stone pier, standing upright in the air, with the top standing on a pillar. There was often cloud surrounding it. Opposite the cloud stone pier was the Qiping Stone, slender and standing alone for more than ten feet, with a horizontal stone covering it, shaped like a chessboard. They then went to Duige Wei Lu, which was the place where Mr. Tao Lan Ting of the Ming Dynasty read books, opposite the former residence of Tao Wenjian Gong's Shi Kui Mountain House. The inside of the cave was suddenly bright and open, with cave islands standing in staggered rows, some like toads, some like elephant trunks, with a landscape similar to Wulingyuan. Lu Master Shen Keming showed the books and paintings he had collected to his companions, making them reluctant to let go. In the evening, they returned to the city, and the Silk Industry Bank's sub-manager borrowed the Commercial Council to hold a public banquet. After the banquet, they were divided into two hotels, Jianhu and Longshan. The next day, they hired a boat and were towed by a steamer to Yuling. The temple was newly built and more magnificent than before. The statue of Da Yu held a jade tablet and stood upright, about ten feet long, making people feel solemn and respectful. Everyone took off their hats and bowed. In front of the hall, they asked Mr. Sun, the director of the Guanzhen Photo Studio, to take a group photo of the group members. Then they visited places such as the Feiyin Spring and Bianshi Pavilion. The spring water was clear and flowed continuously, and they all scooped it up to drink, and it tasted very sweet and cool. The pavilion had a stone button, more than five feet high, which was said to be a tool for water control. It had been smoothed by people's stroking and had red tendons, resembling Han jade. There was a stele on the left of the temple, written by Zhang Taiyan, detailing the merits of Da Yu's water control and the details of this reconstruction, with words such as "If China is not destroyed, the virtue will be widely spread, as if in the Divine Land, no one can compare for a hundred generations." In the afternoon, they went to the banquet of the County Chamber of Commerce. To leave a souvenir, Huang Binhong, who was seventy-one years old, was publicly elected to write the preface, and Xie Gongzhan, Wang Jiyuan, and others drew pictures, entitled "Following the Sound of the Xiuxi," and listed the names of the people of the time. Shaoxing has been opening up streets, improving bridges, facilitating transportation, and its commerce has been becoming more prosperous in recent years, with a thriving atmosphere. In the same capital city, although my He also has a Xing character in its name, the emerging businesses are not as good as those of Shaoxing. When they returned to Hangzhou in the evening, they felt that their teeth and cheeks were still fragrant, because the dishes at this banquet were all rare, such as chicken waist, which is the kidney of a castrated chicken, with a tender and fresh taste. Xidan, also named Zanyunlong, is a live egg that has been half-incubated into a chick but has not yet grown hair. It is unique to Shaoxing and cannot be found elsewhere.

Children's Day and the National Goods Movement 244

— Baling

Today is the universally observed "Children's Day." The reporter feels that it is very meaningful to discuss the relationship between children and the promotion of the national goods movement during "Children's Day." Therefore, I have seized this topic to express some shallow views as follows:

We know that children are the future masters of the country and the pillars of society. The future national fortune of our Republic of China depends entirely on the children of today to take responsibility. In particular, we hope that the parents who are responsible for educating children, as well as the teachers in schools, will take on this training responsibility in advance, so that there will be great hope. These are some simple reasons that everyone understands and no one will deny.

Now, let's put aside other issues for the time being and focus on the national goods movement. I believe that most of the responsibility also rests with the children, because the minds of children are pure and their emotions are passionate. In the pure minds and passionate emotions of children, instilling education to promote national goods and training habits to use national goods, I believe that the results will be very great and effective. Therefore, I sincerely hope that the teachers who pay attention to children's education will also work hard in this area.

This year is the "Student National Goods Year" designated by various groups. Children are part of the student population, and their responsibility for promoting national goods is naturally greater than in previous years. However, most of the actions of children can be said to be passive. They do what adults tell them to do. For example, when it comes to purchasing supplies, adults like to buy from foreign stores. What power do children have to stop them? Even if they understand that buying foreign goods is wrong, they can only understand it in their hearts. Therefore, if we want to train children to buy Chinese goods, the first step is for the parents, elder brothers, teachers, and guardians to set a good example for them to see, which will be effective. However, if there is only lip service and contradictory facts, the effect of promoting national goods will be minimal. Therefore, I hope that on this "Children's Day" that is universally observed throughout the country, on the one hand, we will explain the meaning of promoting national goods, the reasons for buying national goods, and the aspects of promoting national goods to the lovely and dear children, item by item, so that children know that promoting national goods and using national goods are things that children themselves should do, an obligation that should be fulfilled. Once this concept is formed, children will have a deep understanding of national goods, and when they grow up, they will naturally achieve the goal of not wearing anything but national goods, not using anything but national goods, and not eating anything but national goods. When that time comes, our Chinese national goods movement will achieve great success and great achievements.

Taking advantage of today's "Children's Day," I sincerely offer some of my opinions and ask everyone to pay attention and do some work for the national goods movement.

Time flies like a white horse flashing past a crack, and the annual Children's Day has arrived again! Everyone knows that children are the future masters of the country. A Vernacular Poem 246

— Yang An

Children, children, remember that the national crisis is severe. The people are impoverished, wealth is exhausted, and the nation's strength is depleted.

A batch of imported goods empties our silver reserves. Don't just complain about bad harvests, don't just blame the old farmers. It's a thousand times wrong, ten thousand times inexcusable, to have let the word "modern" become so widespread. You want to be fashionable, I want to stand out, ultimately making the dumping of foreign goods successful.

This year is the Students' National Goods Year, don't be deaf and dumb anymore.

Little friends, rise together, work hard and diligently.

From now on, in what you eat, what you wear, and what you use, only choose domestic goods.

Persuade everyone you meet, sound the alarm everywhere, save the nation's strength, revitalize the nation, all depend on the children.

This little vernacular poem is especially written to be read to children on Children's Day of the Students' National Goods Year. Children, you are all very ambitious and determined. My own eight-year-old daughter, ever since I told her to use domestic goods, always asks her mother when she's getting dressed, "Is this Chinese made?" When she's eating something, she always asks her mother, "Is this foreign made?" If she hears it's foreign, she won't wear it or eat it, and she throws a tantrum until we buy her Chinese made goods. People share the same sentiments, hearts share the same reason. Thinking about it, I know all children are like this. So, parents, if you read this poem to them, they will certainly be overjoyed and willing to take on this responsibility on their little shoulders. It's true that if we want to see the day that domestic goods flourish, we must rely on children's firm resolve.

Notes from a Visit

A Record of the Opening Ceremony of the Invincible Soap Factory 247

— Yi Min

—A Good News Story Amidst the Economic Downturn—

The Invincible Soap Factory has opened! In this year when industry and commerce are experiencing a severe economic downturn, it is probably not excessive to have such a relatively gratifying event to cheer everyone up.

Before discussing the opening, I should first talk about the origin of this factory.

Seeing the four characters "Invincible Soap," I believe readers will definitely think of "Invincible Tooth Powder." Yes, this Invincible Soap Factory was jointly established by Mr. Tianxu Wosheng, the inventor of Invincible Tooth Powder, and Mr. Weng Rongbing's family industrial cooperative. Mr. Weng is a soap-making expert, and the family industrial cooperative also had the intention of adding soap manufacturing. Thus, the Invincible Soap Factory was born very smoothly.

The factory is located on West Sports Association Road in the Jiang District. It is a newly built, modern two-story building. The lower floor is the manufacturing department and warehouse, and the upper floor is the packaging room. Before the opening ceremony, I took a trip with the receptionist. Because the time was too short and I am an amateur, I felt like Grandma Liu visiting the Grand View Garden, finding everything new and strange, but understanding nothing. However, according to the person leading my tour, those machines are the most modern. At that moment, I truly felt as happy as if we had recovered the lost territory of the Northeast!

On that day, there were approximately five hundred guests in attendance, including female guests and even foreign guests - Westerners. It was truly a grand and lively occasion. First, Mr. Tianxu Wosheng unveiled the factory and gave a brief report. Next, Mayor Wu's representative, Mr. Li Dachao, delivered an address, followed by speeches from four or five other guests. Below are some fragments that have not yet faded from my memory.

The most noteworthy person was Mr. Tianxu Wosheng. That day, Mr. Chen was truly radiant, exuding a spring-like atmosphere amidst the bright spring sunshine. He humbly asked the guests to provide feedback on the factory's products at any time. He also excitedly hoped that China would no longer have foreign soap. In short, Mr. Chen that day truly seemed to have regained his youth.

Li Dachao's speech on behalf of Mayor Wu was naturally worthy of attention. He felt gratified that the establishment of the Invincible Factory had a great relationship with the prosperity of the city center, and he expressed that the municipal government would definitely provide the factory with various conveniences and support!

Among the speeches by the guests, the words of Mr. Cheng Shouchong, the General Manager of the Shanghai Mechanized Domestic Goods Factory Federation, are also worth noting. First, in a rather amusing tone, he predicted that the Invincible Soap Factory would have unlimited development, the reason being that Mr. Tianxu Wosheng is a senior figure in the domestic industrial sector, and Mr. Weng is a rare soap-making expert in China. Now that the two are working together, it's truly like a peony with green leaves, complementing each other. From now on, the Chinese market will no longer have imported soap, which is something that can be predicted. Secondly, he believed that the Invincible Factory's complete equipment, modern machinery, and meticulous material selection are rare in China, which should be a gratifying thing in today's industrial sector. Thirdly, he expressed sympathy for the establishment of the Invincible Factory in the Chinese area, because although the concessions are also our territory, they are still subject to their restrictions everywhere. Therefore, he believed that the establishment of the Invincible Factory in the Jiang District has at least two meanings: in a passive aspect, it can avoid various unreasonable restrictions in the concessions; in an active aspect, it is helping the government to complete the prosperity of Zhabei.

"National...Goods..." The whistle emitted an echo that seemed to shout out "National Burden." We walked out of the "National Goods" Invincible Soap Factory amidst the echo of "National Goods."

Quickly Create New Domestic Stationery 248

— Xiao Bai

No one can deny that the "economic aggression" of imperialism in our country's market can be described as meticulous, exhausting all the "plundering" and "extracting" capabilities. We know that in the huge trade deficit over the years, there are entire batches of grain, large amounts of wool fabrics, rayon, etc. But, everyone seems to be very vague, unaware that there are also millions of dollars of imported stationery - these daily necessities consumed by general intellectuals - also infiltrating the entire society in every possible way. This is such a terrible fact. This year is the "Students' National Goods Year," and how should we try to make up for this deficiency, eliminate this number, and solve the most important stationery problem in education? It is the most important work of this year.

However, what we should pay attention to at the present stage is that the trend of the times is constantly evolving, and the items needed by a society are also changing to adapt to certain needs. Therefore, at present, there are many new stationery items in our country that cannot yet be manufactured domestically. If we can find ways to avoid them and use domestic goods, it would be best. However, the reality is definitely not that simple. Old writing brushes and Huizhou ink are already being phased out in various special situations. For example, invoices used by domestic goods manufacturers and companies still require pencils and carbon paper. How can we replace pencils with writing brushes in English classes in schools? In view of this factual need, we can therefore firmly shout out the slogan "Quickly Create New Domestic Stationery."

As far as I know, domestic goods manufacturers who can already manufacture new stationery include DAHUA Pencils and MINSHENG Factory's red and blue inks. Mr. Pan Yangyao's Zhongnan Industrial Cooperative, which he founded last year, was the first to create fountain pen barrels that are beautiful, sturdy, and far superior to imported ones. This is of course the best phenomenon for the future of domestic stationery. We can continue to work hard and bury ourselves in our work. Although new stationery is not yet complete (such as nibs, paper, etc., for which there may be no domestic substitutes), in the near future, we can always achieve our wishes.

In short, we can draw the following conclusion regarding the stationery problem: "Within the possible range, we must try our best to use domestic goods and strive to promote new domestic stationery. But, what we still have hope for is that people in the domestic goods industry will quickly formulate an overall plan and create new domestic stationery to meet the needs of society. Do not hesitate or wait and see, and sit back and wait for foreigners' economic domination."

Special Article (Part 1)

How to Save Industry and Commerce? 250

— Huang Yanpei

Speaking of this, some people will definitely suspect that those without capital, how can they help? It should also be investigated what kind of capital is most needed. In my opinion, first, for any enterprise, the preliminary plan is the most important. The seeds of success or failure may have been planted in the business plan long ago. However, with a reasonable plan, it must be implemented faithfully according to the plan. If changes in the situation are discovered, the plan should be quickly revised. Like fighting a war, you must be brave and also have wisdom. Second, since the work purpose belongs to business, the records and accounting of numbers must be accurate. This is the importance of accounting. Many industrial and commercial institutions have sloppy accounting. Because the accounting is not done clearly, they do not necessarily know where the money is being made, and they do not know why they are losing money. Fraud is also easy. In this situation, victory is accidental, and failure is inevitable. If someone lends money without paying attention to the unreasonableness of my plan or my failure to implement the plan, and lends money to help my business without paying attention to the sloppy accounting system I adopt, such lending is no different from waste, and even no different from deliberately increasing the borrower's debt that cannot be repaid. I think if the purpose is narrowly to lend money, everything can be ignored except for lending. Now that the purpose is to provide relief, while helping people with capital, at least you must also advise them on two points: the basic business conditions, what is the plan, and the main business tools, whether the accounting is appropriate or not. This is helping people with good intentions. You must not misunderstand it with other meanings. Looking at it with a broader perspective, to truly save China's crisis, the various organizations, from the government to the society, must all move towards soundness and form a solid national strength, be qualified to coordinate with the enemy to resist and at the same time be qualified to coordinate with people's goodwill, and when I think of the harm of economic aggression by various countries to our country to this extent, the annual trade deficit is tens of millions of yuan, how to break out of the encirclement, only by fundamentally reorganizing the national industry and commerce and helping them to form a sound organization, each industrial and commercial enterprise, has a sound organization; each kind of industry and commerce, has a sound organization; the entire industry and commerce, has a sound organization, manufacturing can be refined, costs can be reduced, transportation can be practical, sales can be promoted, industry and commerce can have vitality, and the country can also have life. But to help industry and commerce, you must find a suitable opportunity. This is the right time!
