Free Talk

Prospects for Children's Happiness on Children's Day 251

— Zhong Yuan

The twentieth century is a century that has expanded children's rights through the women's rights movement. Ellen Key simply calls it the "Century of the Child." This can be proven by the calls for promoting children's happiness in various countries and the formation of various undertakings for children's happiness. In China, there are regulations for Children's Day and Children's Year, and there are also organizations for children's happiness associations and childcare undertakings in various places. All these phenomena can be said to be a surge in the high tide of the world's children's happiness movement. The tumbling of the waves is only one side of the superficial phenomenon of the flowing water. As for the silt and stagnant water at the bottom of the water and the jagged rocks lying across it. These are often neglected by people who appreciate the Jiangchao. However, in fact, if the silt is not cleared and the rocks are not removed, the water flow will not be able to discharge smoothly, and those so-called tides are only a flash in the pan. The children's happiness movement in China seems to be able to symbolize this.

In the noisy city, every Children's Day, one organization holds an infant health competition; another place is specially opened for children, providing entertainment at no cost; some exhibit educational supplies for happy children; some give children sweet candies. So, on this day, in the streets, in the entertainment places, in the institutions that host or also operate children's education undertakings, we can encounter groups of children. The expressions on their faces are all "smiling" and "excited." So generally adults admire that the children of this era have indeed gained immense happiness. This is one side of the children's happiness movement, which is also a side commonly seen by happy people in the happiness movement.

What about the other side? I must first introduce what I saw with my own eyes:

"...At dusk, I went out of school for dinner and passed by the Taishi Bridge, when I suddenly heard a peddler shouting, his voice was so miserable and the name of the thing he was selling seemed unfamiliar. A companion talked to him and found out that what he was shouting was selling children. A passer-by asked the gender of the children he was selling, and the seller replied: 'There are boys and there are girls,' because the basket he was carrying contained his son in the front and his daughter in the back. Someone felt sorry for him and gave him money, and advised him to take both children home, and the seller thanked him with tears. He said that his fields and houses were flooded, and his wife drowned. If he sells the two children, he can still beg for food to live, otherwise he will stay together and wait to die... "March 15, 18th year

This kind of selling people is not only a local and temporary phenomenon.

When the entire rural economy collapsed to a sharp point, the farmers had sold the land, sold the furniture, and finally sold their wives and children. Children who are sold are either slaves or maids or prostitutes. Here, what we see is only the wailing of children, and we do not see the happiness of children.

Every day, as soon as the east shows the fish-white dawn, the ruthless factory siren has issued an emergency assembly order. Among the ranks of adult workers who go to work, many children participate in the same journey. Although they are greedy for sweet sleep, and although they need sufficient sleep. But at this time, they have to wipe their sleepy eyes and rush to the factory. As for life in the factory, according to the Labor Yearbook, the life of apprentices in a woolen mill is as follows:

"Children who are developing work for 13 to 14 hours a day, and their living and eating conditions are extremely poor. The room is full of wool dust and debris. Most of the apprentices have lung diseases and follicular conjunctivitis... They have not received education and have no opportunity to study. Although charitable organizations have tried their best to promote and enable them to receive general education for one or two hours a day, they have failed to realize it due to the opposition of the owners."

In China's 1930 Factory Law, although there is a deadline for "men and women under the age of 14 who have been working in factories before the promulgation of the Factory Law shall submit the names, native places, ages, dates of entry, types of work and nature of work of the workers to the competent authorities for verification within two months after the implementation of the Factory Law." But most manufacturers turned a blind eye, how can they understand the suffering of child labor? Therefore, most of the children who go to work in factories due to family economic pressure only have the attacks of diseases and suffering, and do not see the joy of laughter.

Some children often wander around street corners, and many children come to garbage cans to pick up waste goods. People sometimes curse that these children must not know the importance of literacy or that they are incorrigible and cannot be cultivated. This is somewhat unjust. Because the current schools are really "standing on the walls of the palace for several feet," which are unattainable. In particular, the better primary schools cost dozens of yuan a year, and when registering for school, if there is no acquaintance with the school authorities or the request is not strong enough, they are still "looking at its walls" and have no opportunity to be educated. According to the Ministry of Education's statistics in the 19th year, there were 41 million school-age children in China. There were 7 million students and 34 million dropouts. So most of the children are excluded from cultural influence. The enjoyment of culture is the source of happiness in life. Since most Chinese children are like this, they only have the pity of becoming increasingly ignorant, and they do not have the right to intellectual standards.

All the above-mentioned malformed phenomena that accompany economic relations. When society evolves to the current stage, they are especially "too numerous to count." In short, they all represent the dark side of the children's happiness movement. The facts on this dark side are equal to the silt and rocks in the running water. It hinders the development of the entire children's happiness movement.

If the movement we are advocating is not only for loving apple-like small faces that are lively and vigorous, not only for seeking talents and rejoicing in their "malleability," not only for "reviving the family reputation" to "glorify the family," but for paying attention to the education of the entire Chinese child, which holds back the development of the entire national spirit. Then, the first thing we should pay attention to is not to stand and watch the tide and applaud it, but to find ways to dredge and remove the silt and rocks that block the flowing water.

24, 44.

Month 252

— Yecao

The warmth of spring is still the same as in previous years.

But Huangzhuang is not the same as before!

In the spring of previous years, at the south end of that open space, the Land God Temple located at the intersection always had lively incense fairs. People were like bees, in groups, crowding around, as if swimming in pleasant circumstances, everyone had a heart of indescribable joy. Old women held their grandchildren and came to the fair from remote places. Women usually rarely left their homes, but at this moment, they were putting on rouge in front of the mirror, braiding red braids for their daughters, and then, taking long benches, three or five of them together, went out so awkwardly.

But what about Huangzhuang now?

After two years of famine attacks, people can no longer resist life. A kind of terror built on hunger makes young people have no nostalgia for their homes. They began to flee to that ideal blessed land!

Day by day, young people ran away as much as they could. What was left were the old men and women who were unwilling to leave their hometown, and their young children. When the young people kindly advised them that staying in their hometown for a long time would make them starve, Father Huang raised his voice and shouted rudely:

"Is it that easy? You should also think carefully, even though there is little property, it was always passed down by the ancestors. If you leave, where are you going to get it!"

"If you don't leave, what are you going to eat, drink the wind!"

"Hmph! Kid! Tree bark, can't you eat it? And tree leaves."

"Hiss!" The young man hissed anxiously.

No matter how stubborn the old man was, these young people finally left their homes one by one.

The old people eked out their dying days, eating one meal a day—thin porridge made of tree bark crumbs and flour—with their grandchildren. Life is long, but the tree bark has a time when it will be eaten up; this, first of all, caused panic among the old people.

People are ultimately smart, and often when unsolvable problems come, they will come up with solutions. One day, the old woman looked at Father Huang disappointedly:

"What should we do when the tree bark is finished?"

"Eat tree leaves."

"What if the leaves are all picked?"

"Water algae, there are a lot of them in the river, people don't know about it!"

Yes, after many days, Father Huang brought back a package of water algae. He walked with special energy, showing a smile that had not been seen for months; he seemed to feel very proud in his heart, at least his family could have a full meal this time, because he had such a big package in his hand.

Unfortunately, the next day the whole family swelled up as thick as their necks and faces, and their tongues were stiff, making it difficult to speak. One grandson innocently shouted:

"Grandma, your face is like a moon, round, so is Grandpa's; what's wrong?"

"Hmm!" She hummed softly, biting her trembling lower lip tightly.

Water algae are poisonous!

By the Cao'e River 253

— Qian Dong

It has been five years. Five years ago, with what state of mind did I cross this Cao'e River? Thinking back, I truly have a sense of past and present!

It was a winter morning. The sun had just smiled, and soon the sky became gloomy again, and the wind was more ferocious than wild beasts, roaring terrifyingly.

Walking to the riverbank, it began to rain and snow. The mud road was very slippery, and if you were not careful, you would fall. The ferry was lonely and silent in the rain. The wind, rain, and snow played a lonely tune, and the Cao'e River slowly sang the elegy of the exiles. We crossed this small river dimly with emotions that were more sentimental than the exiles.

Now, the peach blossoms on the riverbank are in full bloom, the willows have sprouted tender green buds, the light yellow river water is constantly flowing eastward, and the golden sun is all over the mountains and rivers. And me, I am still crossing the Cao'e River with all the sentimental emotions I had five years ago.

I let my sight search as freely as possible. I want to explore the traces of changes in the past five years in this small world; however, I am disappointed. I can't see any changes in the past five years. People are still bustling, rowing boats, drawing river water, and porters are still signaling to me with drunken faces with their rough poles in groups: "Do you want a porter?" The peddlers along the coast are still shouting noisily, and the people going in and out of the small restaurants still seem to be the same Shaoxing men who curse "Ma Du Bi" as soon as they open their mouths. I even feel that the children playing stone marbles on the river beach are still the same group as five years ago!

However, the things that I personally experienced before have changed too drastically.

The second train arrived. I got into the carriage and closed my eyes tightly. I don't want to see anything anymore. I am afraid of finding traces of our past in the fine sand.

Doo! The car is moving. I lowered my head, wanting to throw all the past behind the car. Unintentionally, I actually recited an ancient poem: "When I left in the past, the rain and snow were heavy, but now I come, the willows are gentle."

The wheels rubbed against the rails, squeaking and squeaking, and the locomotive wailed. I pricked up my ears to listen, and the Cao'e River gradually disappeared into the morning light!

Gleanings (2) (Continued) 254

— Wo Pu

(4) The Zhongshan Wolf

Kang Hai's "Mr. Dongguo and the Zhongshan Wolf" miscellaneous drama was written to criticize Li Mengyang and vent his own resentment. It was probably not based on factual events. At the same time, Ma Zhongxi, who had also suffered at the hands of Liu Jin, wrote a "Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf," using prose to express the same story. Niu Xiu, in his *Gu Yu*, raised objections to Ma's work, as seen in the "Jade Sword Error" entry:

"The 'Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf' was written by Xie Liang of the Song Dynasty. Although it was a playful piece, it must have been alluding to something at the time, but he did not want to state it explicitly, using this to vent his anger. Yu Jianzun heard it said, 'When Li Xianji was imprisoned, Liu Jin urgently wanted to kill him and wrote a slip of paper, saying, "Save me, Dui Shan!" His family went to tell Kang, who immediately mounted his horse and rushed to Jin's gate to plead for him. The next day, he was released. Later, Xianji became jealous and harmful to Dui Shan. Ma Zhongxi wrote the "Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf" to satirize Xianji.' Dui Shan's rescue of Xianji was originally not in the hope of repayment from Xianji. Even if Xianji had resentment, how could it be as extreme as the "Zhongshan Wolf"? Moreover, its literary style is rich and flourishing, which people of the Song Dynasty could not have done. Ma Dongtian had regrets about Xianji and wrote this to scold him, so it was thought that it was written by Dongtian. Ming Wenying still followed this, but he did not examine it deeply."

Dong Ji's *Complete Catalog and Abstracts of Qu Opera*, Volume 5, records the Zhongshan Wolf entry. Examining the full text of the Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf, it also says it was written by Xie Liang of the Song Dynasty, with a note at the end saying: "According to the *Record Compilation*, it was written by Ma Zhongxi." The abstract author probably received inspiration from Niu's *Gu Yu*. It is also possible? Niu's saying of "writing to scold each other" is a possible explanation, but Xie Liang's person seems to be unknown. Neither book mentioned it. In short, whether attributing the Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf to a Song Dynasty writer is accurate or not will be put aside for the moment. The spread of this "ungratefulness" story should have a much earlier history.

In the table of contents, the abstract marks the author of the Zhongshan Wolf miscellaneous drama as Ma Zhongxi! This article examines and says:

"People at the time used it to criticize Li Mengyang. (Omission) People at the time wrote the Zhongshan Wolf miscellaneous drama to satirize him, or it is said that it was written by Hai."

The author of the abstract did not definitively attribute the author to Dui Shan, only repeatedly saying "people at the time," and did not involve Ma at all. This is probably because the abstract quoted the Biography of the Zhongshan Wolf, noting "it was written by Ma Zhongxi, etc." The editors misread this, thinking that it referred to the miscellaneous drama, thus leading to this error, without examining it. (The End)

A Scene of the Common People 255

Mr. Juqing (6) 256

— Ke Ling

After hesitating for a few days, Zhang Wencan finally came, followed by Widow Zhang wearing a moon-white bamboo cloth vest. Both mother and son looked very gloomy, as if something unexpected had happened.

Letting her sit down modestly, the first thing she said was:

"Mr., we, A'can, have come to say goodbye to you. He's leaving tomorrow to go to the city to learn business."

"Oh!" Mr. Juqing answered with only one word, as if he had heard a thunderbolt out of the blue.

"Yes, to learn business in a cloth shop in the city. It's his uncle who arranged it." She sighed softly and continued, "The child is so young, and he's going to a strange place far away from home. I'm all alone at home, so I'm really worried. Originally, according to my idea, he should have learned more from you, Mr., for another three or four years, and then go out when he's seventeen or eighteen. That would be much better! But his uncle said: It's difficult to find business opportunities now, so it's better for him to go out early if he has the chance... Alas, it's just that A'can is unlucky; his father died early!"

Tears hung on her anemic face as she looked sadly at her son.

Wencan stood aside with red eyes, staring blankly.

"A real man will have to go out sooner or later. A'can is quite sensible at home, so I'll just let him go. But it's good to be at home for a thousand days, but it's hard to be away for even one day. It's always hard to eat someone else's rice while learning business!"

The students stopped reading aloud, and eight or nine pairs of small eyes stared at them, making the air eerily quiet. After a long while, Mr. Juqing comforted Widow Zhang, saying:

"Don't worry. Wencan is a very sensible child. He'll definitely be successful in the future. Don't worry!"

"Really? Thank you for your kind words, Mr.! A'can, you must 'endure and win.' Be ambitious, and don't forget what the teacher said!" She turned back to the teacher solemnly and said, "In the future, if we have letters to exchange, we'll have to trouble you, Mr."

Wencan nodded, unable to speak. The tears that filled his eyes finally burst forth and streamed down his face.

After Mr. Juqing saw the mother and son off, he himself almost shed tears.

Of course, Mr. Juqing's private school was not the only one in such a miserable situation; all the other private schools were the same, and most were even worse off than his. Strangely enough, the sacred educational cause in this town has not only failed to attract students and create a blossoming field of talent but has also resembled a dying lamp with little oil, dim and bleak, relying only on the faint light of a single wick to support the dilapidated situation.

At the same time, the common enemy of the private schools in the town—the school—is also in a somewhat precarious state.

At the end of the first month, less than half a month after the district elementary school opened, news of their brewing trouble spread throughout the town.

The district elementary school is a notoriously poor school. The principal is often concurrently held by a school board member in name only. The three teachers are usually unemployed young people drifting around the local area or colorful characters who have drifted back from other places, who, when asked, may have some connection to the school board member; occasionally, there is a teacher from another place, often a scholar of the disheveled and bohemian type. As for salary, the principal receives twelve dollars a month, and the teachers receive five to eight dollars. Every year during the winter and summer vacations, after school is dismissed, the teachers often have two or three months' worth of salary unpaid, sitting around and waiting in vain. Those who become teachers usually do not enter this school unless they are at their wit's end.

However, there are people who are enthusiastic about education, and quite a few want to become school board members of the district elementary school.

*Shen Bao* Local Supplement

Not a Trivial Matter 257

— Chen

Reading the number three newspaper, within the so-called yellow news, suicide events can be summarized as follows: (1) Mrs. Zhang, a Shanghai woman, whose husband has been unemployed for more than a year. The family's livelihood depends on her work at the Meifeng Silk Weaving Factory in the United States. However, her income is very meager, and there is often a danger of running out of food. Thinking about the long future ahead, how can she maintain it? Out of resentment, she suddenly had the thought of ending her life. She secretly swallowed opium and committed suicide. (2) Ying San'er from Changzhou, who worked in the iron cart business, suddenly committed suicide by taking poison at the Yong'an Hotel on McEnne Road. In a suicide note to his mother-in-law, he said that he was heavily in debt and unable to repay it, so he had no choice but to do this. (3) (Seven-world legend?) The young man Yue Rufeng, due to economic difficulties, actually planned to die. He went alone to the Southeast Hotel on North Mud City Bridge and secretly took a heavy dose of Lysol poison and committed suicide. (4) Lin Su, a student at the Customs Taxation School from Guangdong, was inherently slow, so he failed every exam. He was usually depressed. Recently, another small exam was approaching, causing him to overuse his brain and have a nervous breakdown. Fearing that he would not be able to graduate and hold a position in the future, he became more stimulated every day and suddenly became weary of life. He took a kitchen knife and slit his throat.

Suicide, this was something that attracted attention a year or two ago. But now, even though these words reveal traces of blood, the general public has become numb to it. What does it matter if a few people commit suicide? However, recently, this trend of suicide has shifted from the middle and upper social classes to the general public, from individual cases of disappointment in love or humiliation to large-scale occurrences with economic hardship as the root cause. If we observe the frequency of suicide and examine its more serious social significance, then we must say that it is indeed not a trivial matter.

Just as the entire situation is heading into danger, China's national economy has reached the point of being "forced to hang itself." From rural bankruptcy to industrial decline, under these circumstances, following the farmers in the countryside killing their children and committing suicide as a family, this "Paris of the East," Shanghai, is also entering this dead end. Store closures and factory shutdowns are almost "commonplace." What will happen to these many laid-off and unemployed people? Many people whose opportunities for survival have been deprived and who have not seen the root cause of this are sacrificing themselves to this unknown weariness of life!

Therefore, the seriousness of suicide lies not in the individual's "great liberation." It symbolizes the suicide of the national economy and the suicide of the national destiny. To try to salvage the situation by relying on some kind of economic support from others, hoping to obtain a bit of "rain and dew," is not this method of drinking poison to quench thirst tantamount to suicide?

Sparks in the Spring Fields 258

— Kemin

("Wildfires cannot be extinguished, the spring breeze blows and they are reborn." In March, the piles of ashes in the fields are full of sighs and longings for the past generation. They also include the depression of young people and the lost love of young widows. All of this drifts into the sky with the paper butterflies.

Those who have died have finally died, and forever. And those who are destined not to die will eventually climb into the earth holes helplessly. The posture of life and procreation is formed in such a way. The convergence of the stream of life is the desolate yellow earth.

And those who can truly fight against the iron laws of nature, it can only be said that they are the wildfires in front of the tombs during the Cold Food Festival. They flicker constantly and stubbornly with the breath of the spring breeze, struggling, as if to proudly boast to the dead spirits in the earth holes--flickering, and then flickering again.

The sparks in the spring fields are terrifying!)

When I arrived at the Tan Family Lane with the cart driver, I could already see a touch of spring in the wild fields. Living... I drifted far away from the land I loved, and this time, when I saw the spring in the small villages of the north again, my memory of the wild fields was decorated with many new graves and mounds.

"So many graves!" Yes, I understand that the people of my homeland, who I had in my thoughts, all silently (?) climbed down into the yellow earth under the misfortune of the troubled times. But what I remember are those honest, trustworthy lines engraved on the old, dark faces.

The cart driver clicked his tongue and, with an indignant and garrulous expression, cracked his whip hard on the back of the animal, turned to look at me, and made a sound of "hee," like a sigh, but also like a bitter smile—

"Sir, your family is blessed, so you don't know much about it. This year, the people in the countryside are all unlucky. Some have died, some have slipped away. The rest are weak and can't run far. They can't leave the small river and the patch of sun in front of their old houses. So they are determined to live each day without knowing what the next will bring, until the day they die."

The spring fields are not suitable for narrating unpleasant events. Moreover, aren't those piles of new mounds and the ashes of paper money in the wild fields telling me enough? So, I wanted to be silent.

But the old cart driver's past suffering simply could not hold his tongue—this was really not easy. He took a breath and then clumsily spit out a string of painful sounds—

"The countryside has become unrecognizable in recent years—the soldiers fought a battle, followed by a series of famine years. Times are getting worse every day. Life in the countryside is not easy... The people in the town who sell rice, oil, soy sauce, and groceries can't make a living either. They have all 'let go of the horses'— During the season of the great floods in the autumn, many old folks died, many died..."

"The men have all slipped away, leaving their wives at home to starve—what kind of talk is this? Like that, the prettier ones hook up with peddlers from out of town. What can you say about this world! When their husbands died, they burned some wildflowers in the fields. That's how it is: the dead are dead, and those who have left will never return."

Listening and talking, the person was listless, and the cart dragged its wooden wheels on the muddy road like a rat gnawing on something, making an uncomfortable noise. This time, the shadow of my homeland truly appeared before my eyes, but what a dark shadow!

The sparks in the spring fields are endless, and in the distance, there are piles of paper ashes with black smoke rising. Spring sweeps by, but endlessly sparks little bits of fire, like representing the suffering of a group of people, and also like symbolizing another kind of endless depression that crosses the barren land of the north.

This year's Cold Food Festival is not suitable for spring outings. The sparks in the fields are brewing another kind of unpleasant meaning: "The dead are dead, and those who have left will never return."

Daughter of Phoenix 259

— Xin Er

Starting from the foot of Hanshan Mountain along the banks of the E'xi River, you must struggle to climb the high mountains and steep ridges all day long, pass through countless desolate valleys and deep forests where there are no people, before you can drag your sore steps into Phoenix Village from Puwei Ridge at dusk when the birds return to the forest!

In the middle of the overlapping mountains, you can move forward and listen to the low奏 from the secluded deep forest and the gurgling water, suddenly flash to see a beautiful and clear leisure of the human world, making people suddenly drunk! This is Phoenix Mountain, Phoenix Village. More than ten years ago, it was almost completely isolated from the outside world.

The women in this deep mountain, like the Peach Blossom Spring, are very special. Later, the people of the first county town called them "Daughters of Phoenix," which has a very rare meaning. Maybe it's because the mountains are beautiful and the water is clear, and the scenery is too clean? Although the women are extremely hardworking, they are blown by the wind, sun, and rain all year round, but their skin is still delicate, white, clean, simple and innocent. They have inherited customs from their ancestors for hundreds of years, and there has never been such a thing as foot binding. Unmarried girls wear a long braid. Married women must get up at five o'clock every morning and spend an hour putting on makeup. Their hair is smeared with a lot of tea oil and combed into a complex and huge machine-like shape, inserted with many ornaments, and the back is combed into a protruding large axe-like shape, which is very strange. Moreover, as long as they step out of the boudoir, in the family, or in the farmland, they must cover their heads with a square, thick, black-blue cloth, and red silk thread is sewn on the green edge of the cloth. Both ears must be pierced

Page 22

with small holes and hung with earrings. At any time, the sleeves of the shirt must be the same as the palms of the hands, and the length must cover the knees. This is neither like a cheongsam nor a short shirt. No matter whether it is hot summer or spring, they always wear black cloth clothes as usual, and there will never be a second type of clothing. And I have never seen them wear socks, except on the day they are brides. Wearing shoes is also very rare. They always like to drag a pair of wooden clogs, and even the wooden clogs are taken off as soon as they step into the house. Most of them are barefoot from a distance. Almost every sole of the feet of the daughter-in-law is cracked. Even if they go out to visit guests, it is rare to drag slippers, and it is simply impossible to wear shoes. Some wealthy old ladies are forced by their sons to wear socks, and she will find it very troublesome and annoying.

Almost every family farms. Regardless of the rich or poor, women of wealthy families must also go barefoot to the fields. This is really a strange custom! They are very strong. Not only are all the things in the family done by women, but also the work of planting the fields. Women must work more than men. Moreover, it is the responsibility of women to go to the deep mountains to cut firewood. If men go to the mountains with women, they will be laughed at. There are also many women who go over the mountains to work as coolies. That kind of hard work is truly beyond the reach of any other women. Therefore, the productivity of women is often stronger than that of their husbands. No, she worked hard than others, and the treatment she received was even more bizarre! Her husband is like a young master! But their parents must also make their wives work hard all year round. The husband is like a noble master, and the wife is like a lowly servant. I could not understand how they lived such a husband and wife life when I was young. So what reason makes women like this.

Amateur Mailbox

Sending 300 Easy Characters Table 260

With the Opinions of Bai Hong, Zhang Kunzhai, and Dai Hongxun

Since this column published several letters about easy characters, the editor has received many letters from readers, some of which are about the selected easy characters, added consultation; some are discussing how to promote easy characters, and most are telling us what they know about easy characters. Their enthusiasm for easy characters is admirable, but some readers have not seen all of the 300 easy characters that have been selected, so although they have written dozens of easy characters, in reality, very few of the 300 easy characters have been adopted; some readers have written many easy characters, all of which are already in the 300 characters. Isn't this a waste of many readers' energy and time? At the same time, I have received many letters from readers asking us to publish all of the 300 easy characters in this column every few days for their reference and use. This request cannot be fulfilled because of the limited space in this column. Therefore, in order to remedy the above two things, the editor has asked the Easy Character Promotion Association to print the 300 characters into a table. If readers need to refer to it, please send a one-cent postage and the editor will send a copy. Regarding the letters discussing easy characters, a part of them will be published below:

Bai Hongjun's opinion: After reading several simplified characters listed by Yu Fangjun, the character "垒" is actually a different character, read as "磊," meaning a cannon-fort or a high-fort, and cannot be used as a simplified character for "垒." The simplified character for "垒" should be "垒."

Also, in the 300-character list selected by the Easy Character Promotion Association, "穀" as "谷" and "够" as "勾" are both inappropriate, because "谷" and "勾" have independent meanings of their own. In fact, the simplified character for "穀" is usually written as "槖." The characters "漢" as "汉" and "嘆" as "叹" are not commonly seen. If you change "叹" to "咲," it seems to be more popular. Also, the character "發" as "蕟" is not as good as "発." The character "縣" as "县" is not as good as "" because this kind of drawing only exists in print, and it does not exist in cursive writing. Now, following the editor's intention, I will list the easy characters I know below: 春作 "", 作 "察" 歷作 "厤".

Zhang Kunzhai's suggestion: I am very much in favor of the promotion of easy characters. Now I would like to put forward some opinions and hope that everyone will discuss them.

When we usually write the character "編," we probably all write it as "編," and the same is true for the other characters with the "糹" radical. Everyone can recognize them when they are written. The "言" radical can also be simplified by a few strokes. For example, "詩" is written as "诗" and "誠" as "誠." Changing the "鴻" character with the water radical to "鴻" is also more convenient. I wonder what the gentlemen who advocate easy characters think?

Easy characters written by Dai Hongxun:

Original characters: 本 字 墳 在 藥 賣 鑒 東 協 將 戴 弟

Easy characters: 坆 葯 卖 东 协 将

My Career Introduction

Luo Fengjun, from Shanghai, graduated from Qunzhi University, and has served as secretary, counselor, section chief, etc. in administrative offices, organizations, and groups. He is good at drafting administrative official documents, punctuating official documents, revising laws, and writing books. He is especially good at fine regular script, imitation Song, and art fonts. Those who want to hire him, please send a letter to Xiao Zhenkai, No. 88, Robert Sheng Road.

Zhu Jun, with a high school education level, is willing to serve as an apprentice in a merchant company, a copyist in an agency, or a messenger in a public hall. He has a guarantee and his address is Liu Dasheng, Building 7, upstairs from the small vegetable market on Gongxing Road, Zhabei.

A certain gentleman, from Jiangsu, now wishes to work as a copyist assistant in a company or a messenger in an agency. The salary is not counted, and only food and lodging are required. He has a solid shop guarantee. The address is Liu Dasheng, Building 7, upstairs from the small open market at the intersection of Zhongxing Road and Gongxing Road, Zhabei.

Suzhou Ballad 261

Sun Huiqing and Zhou Huifang

New Sound (1380) 9:30 AM to 10:30 AM

Opening "Lamenting the Battlefield"

Only for fame and profit do they seize military states. Slaughter and killing cycle endlessly. How many heroes and gentlemen. With ambition they want to be kings. But only see the river flowing east. How many famous generals are left? Only to have their bodies wrapped in horsehide and return to their graves. A mound of yellow earth like a steamed bun. When fighting, heaven and earth are dark. Mountains and rivers change color in sorrow. The sound of the reeds and drums is about to end. Brave men each move their spears. A battle divides victory and defeat. How much green blood fills the mountain trees. The lady dreams after midnight. The mournful sound of the night watch drums has not ended. White bones are like mountains, dry for a long time. The setting sun accompanies the years for a long time. Only her hero's blood in the tomb. Protects the people's livelihood with the most excellent merit. I come to mourn alone today. Heaven and earth, mountains and rivers, grass and trees are sad. For thousands of years, we have fought against each other. Everyone shares the same hatred with the enemy. Only then are we worthy of the hero's name.

Classical Prose 263

Wang Shuimei's Donglai Exposition

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Marquis Xi Attacks Zheng (Continued)

He indulges himself in honor, why should I rejoice? He demeans himself in degradation, why should I be angry? The mind is my mind, and it should manage my affairs. How can it spare time to assist the joy of the honored or the anger of the degraded? (End)

Yu Fu Murders Duke Yin

Alas! What corrupts the world's heart for righteousness is the murder of Duke Yin. Profit is what people seek, righteousness is what people shun. If being righteous had no misfortune, people would still be unwilling. How much more if burdened with misfortune? Duke Yin managed a country of a thousand chariots, but he relinquished it to Duke Heng. Duke Heng, in turn, did not appreciate his heart and murdered him. He had the highest integrity, yet he suffered the cruelest misfortune. The world will point to Duke Yin as a warning and avoid speaking of righteousness. What I have heard is different. People all believe that the murder of Duke Yin corrupts the world's heart for righteousness. I alone believe that it can encourage the world's heart for righteousness. Why is this? The murder of Duke Yin was not because he sat idly doing righteousness, but because he did not do enough righteousness.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

The Six Major Stars Awarded by the Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences in 1934 (Part 2) 265

— Huang Yingdai

(2) Subsequent Evaluation

The honorable awards were finally revealed on the night of February 27th. As a result, Clark Gable for "It Happened One Night," Norma Shearer for "The Barretts of Wimpole Street," William Powell for "The Thin Man," Grace Moore for "One Night of Love," Frank Morgan for "Affairs of Cellini," and Claudette Colbert for "It Happened One Night" were awarded, totaling six people, half male and half female.

However, after the announcement, problems arose again. Among the above-mentioned six people, male and female stars, which two's art has reached the highest peak and ranked first?

But this is bound to disappoint you. The Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences not only does not list the order of rankings, but even the results of each person's evaluation among the six people, how many votes they received, will not tell you, and they publish the list in the order of the first letter in each person's English name.

Therefore, we found that in the list, the order of the female stars is Claudette Colbert first, Grace Moore second, and Norma Shearer third.

As for the male stars, Clark Gable is first, Frank Morgan is second, and William Powell is third.

So, in the above list, we cannot identify who is first. Even what method the Academy used to select on the night of February 27th, outsiders do not know. Similarly, which film in the past year can be the representative work of the year.

After this list was announced, what made the people of Hollywood feel surprised was that two actors were awarded for starring in the same film—Clark Gable and Claudette Colbert were both awarded for "It Happened One Night." Since the Academy handled this award, it has never happened that two actors were awarded for one film; this is the first time!

In Film City, the general opinion was that Norma Shearer's performance as Elizabeth Barrett Browning in "The Barretts of Wimpole Street" was enough for her to win the Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences Award for 1934. As a result, they really guessed right. William Powell could at least be included in the initial selection. The collaboration between Gable and Colbert was also considered by anyone to have a chance of winning.

At the same time, on the opposing side, some people were upset about Frank Morgan's award. They all said that Morgan's award was stealing the positions of Constance Bennett and Fredric March. However, some people also thought that Morgan deserved to be selected. Perhaps even Morgan himself would be surprised to see his name on the list!

Columbia originally did not attach importance to the film "One Night of Love" until after the evaluation, when it discovered that there were many reasons for it to be awarded. In this film, Grace Moore's singing and expression reached the highest peak. Therefore, she was able to occupy a seat among the three winning female stars. This film has been listed among the twelve best films of 1934 in Hollywood. The director, Victor Schertzinger, also won an award for this film. People in the art world all recognize that several songs in "One Night of Love" can be called the highest peak of art. (End)

Film Reviews

Review of "A Wicked Woman" 266

— Chan Fei

A Wicked Woman

— Nanjing Screening

Although the original name is titled "Wicked Woman," it actually portrays a virtuous mother and good wife, because the protagonist's killing of her husband in this film is for the sake of her children. Her tireless struggle is also for the sake of her children. In other words, for the so-called happiness of her children, she finally raised her children from a state of hunger and cold to adulthood, earning the status of a good citizen from a bandit. Moreover, she is a woman with a very good conscience. She has a kind nature, so she will never forget that harming her husband is an unforgivable sin in the eyes of God and a heinous crime unforgivable by national law. Therefore, she believes that her children's mistakes are all divine retribution, and she finally acts on it. But because the audience sympathizes with her, in the end, reason, national law, and human sentiment are combined, and she, who should have been sentenced to death, is acquitted. She has fulfilled her oath to God and received amnesty from national law (seemingly joking with the law a bit). In addition, she remarries to her ideal husband. This wicked woman gives people with old ideas a very good impression.

In the feudal era, the protagonist, Naomi, was not necessarily a revolutionary woman. Shooting her husband, struggling hard, supporting herself, and sacrificing herself for the happiness of her descendants. However, this is a superficial observation. If we explore the inner workings of the work more thoroughly, we will inevitably discover the screenwriter's intention to vigorously maintain the old social system. Naomi's killing of her husband is precisely the screenwriter's deeper way to maintain the existence of old morality. She kills her husband because her husband cannot live in poverty, because her husband wants to take risks, and because her husband cannot be a righteous gentleman with a moral conscience. Therefore, she kills her husband precisely to eliminate harm for society and enable her children to become moral people. Naomi in this film is the perfect person in the eyes of the upholders of morality. She is a good mother, and later marrying a newspaper editor will inevitably also make her a good wife. However, she is ultimately an ideal character! It is difficult for us to see authenticity in it.

Now let's look at how the authors (including the director, actors, screenwriters, etc.) create their characters and how they use old-fashioned ideas to move the audience.

On a stormy night, in that small house by the water, the poor man's wife kills her husband. At this critical moment, his son wakes up. She cannot help but endure her frightened heart to comfort the child to sleep, singing a lullaby very lovingly. Soon, she rows a small boat and throws her husband's corpse into the river bottom in the midst of a storm. … This scene, whether it is the sound effects, the acting skills of the new actress Mady Christians, the photography, the director Charles Brabin's grasp of the tension and rapid changes in emotions, or the screenwriter's use of her to show the ruthlessness of killing her husband and immediately show her love for her children, all combine to become a brilliant technical performance.

Later, we hear the protagonist confessing to God, because she wants her daughters to live in sin, waiting for her children to become adults, she vows to turn herself in and atone for her sins. Some time later, she returns from working in the factory. The eldest daughter is cooking, the second daughter is secretly wanting a foreign doll, and the son is washing his younger brother while playing. She immediately urges her daughter to work, urges her son to study, and the bathing of the younger son depicts the peace of the family. After a burst of laughter from the audience, she cruelly burns her second daughter's foreign doll (the second daughter's personality serves as a foreshadowing for her later elopement), followed by her heartbreaking crying, which gives people a great feeling.

Twelve years later, the children have grown up and have their own professions. Here, the mother explains her children's professions and personalities by driving an old car, and also begins to explain her love affair with the newspaper editor who is her son. During the rest time after dinner, the younger son plays the violin, the second daughter plays the piano… filling the family with happiness. After the children go to bed, she and the editor talk very congenially, while depicting her inner sorrow. The second daughter meets her lover at night, and the sorrow of the disabled is portrayed on the younger son's football. … In these places, there are very cinematic depictions. As for the mother and children crying together before leaving home to turn herself in, on the train, and in the courtroom, all of them show technical success.

In all aspects, it shows the authors' proficiency in technology. In order to uphold morality, they vividly portray their ideal perfect person, which precisely illustrates the great power of film works to move people. New ethical films can certainly serve as authentic things for the new era, while old ethical concepts are also fully used as tools for preaching in the old society. Therefore, "A Wicked Woman" is still an extraordinary work.

About "I Was a Spy" 267

— Qing

The war blockbuster "I Was a Spy" is a glorious production of the British Gaoxiang Company. The main actors are Conrad Veidt and Madeleine Carroll, whose reputations have long spread throughout the world. The entire film's plot is based on the history of espionage in the European war, writing about a Belgian woman who, forced by the German army's lewd power, nurses wounded soldiers in a hospital behind German lines. Only the sounds of tragic cries and moans, calling for mothers and seeking children, are unbearable to witness and unbearable to hear. Furthermore, because of the subversion of the country, she is regarded as a daughter of a fallen country. She does not hesitate to sacrifice her own life, secretly serving as a spy, and performs outstanding service for the country. Her ambition and actions are admirable. In addition to the tight plot and profound performances, this film also has various amazing scenes of airplane bombings. It is heard that it has been scheduled to open at the Paris Grand Theatre on Xiafei Road starting this Friday.

"The Fugitive" Now Re-released 268

— Qingyun

The Art China Film Company's great production of this year, the music and song film "The Fugitive," which has been praised by Chinese and foreign newspapers, has been sold out every day and every show since it was released at the Jincheng Grand Theatre on the 21st of last month. Subsequently, because various theaters and production companies in this city had scheduled to hold a meeting at Jincheng on the 31st to welcome Mr. Tao Bosen, our representative attending the Soviet Russian International Film Exhibition, and Jincheng also decided to re-release "Song of the Fishermen" for a few days from that day, "The Fugitive" was temporarily suspended. Now, due to the requests of the majority of the audience, "The Fugitive" has been decided to be re-released at the Jincheng Grand Theatre starting today (4th).

"The Golden Watch" to Begin Filming Soon 269

Cai Chusheng's new work after "New Woman" has been praised by all parties for the script "Human Zoo" he wrote last year, so the Lianhua authorities also plan to have Cai direct and film the play. However, because "Human Zoo" has many actors, and several main characters still need to be found, and the background is mostly in severe winter, it is not suitable to engage in filming at this time. Moreover, after the two factories are concentrated, a new film must be started, so Cai Chusheng decided to put this script aside temporarily. And in the next ten days, he buried himself in work and completed his script "The Golden Watch" (provisional title). Regarding the backbone of this play, it is based on a famous Russian work. However, in order to enhance the dramatic power and suit the national conditions, more excellent supplements are added, making it a very moving film drama. It is expected that this film will greatly benefit children. It is heard that the main characters have been selected as Ge Zozhi, a child prodigy discovered by Lianhua, and Chen Sujuan, who had good results in "New Woman."

Shen Bao Film Special Submission Guidelines 270

This publication is a film publication that assists in the promotion of culture and art. All submissions are welcome, and once published, generous remuneration will be provided.

Once the text is published and paid, the copyright belongs to Shen Bao.

The text in this publication is mainly in vernacular Chinese and must use modern punctuation.

Each submission must be sealed with a stamp, otherwise it will be returned without remuneration.

The space in this publication is limited, so the text should be as short as possible, with each submission limited to around 500 words.

If the submission is a translation, the original work should be attached. English should be omitted if possible.

Unless otherwise stated in advance and return postage is attached, this publication is not responsible for the preservation or return of texts, photos, etc.

Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper, do not write horizontally, and do not use a pencil.

If it is found that one manuscript is submitted to multiple publications, plagiarized, or copied verbatim from instructions, no remuneration will be given.

Film Novel

Elegy of Life (4) 271

— Pei Yuan

Manna's child fell ill with whooping cough, which is highly contagious. Suqiu still took her own child along every day. But as a result, Suqiu's child was unfortunately infected with Manna's child's whooping cough. So when Manna's child recovered, Suqiu's child fell ill. When Suqiu and Meng'ou took their child to the outpatient clinic of Jiren Hospital, they happened to meet Qiao Jie, whom they had not seen for many years. Qiao Jie had also come to treat his wounded right wrist. It turned out that Qiao Jie had left Meng'ou's house when the January 28 Incident broke out. He joined the front line to fight, injured his right wrist, and after the war ended, he was demobilized and wandered the streets. At the same time, they also met Manna and Liu Ying, because Manna's child was discharged from Jiren Hospital on this day. As they were preparing to get into the car, Meng'ou and Suqiu happened to carry their child out of the hospital. When Liu Rong saw Meng'ou, he immediately stepped forward to greet him, making him feel ashamed, embarrassed, and angry. But Manna pretended not to recognize Meng'ou. Although Liu Rong was willing to use his car to send Meng'ou and others back, Meng'ou declined.

On the road, Meng'ou rebuked Suqiu for why she had concealed it from him. Suqiu replied very sadly, "I hate that you wouldn't let me go, so I had to keep it a secret." Meng'ou nodded proudly and said, "What bad luck, to run into this pair of villains today." The disease of Meng'ou and Suqiu's child worsened, but they had no money to hire a doctor to treat him, so they could only watch helplessly as their beloved son groaned on the bed.

In the absence of a rescue method, Meng'ou thought of going to Qiao Jie to find a way. But when Meng'ou found the place where Qiao Jie lived, it was when Qiao Jie was being kicked out by the landlord for not paying the rent. At this time, it was when the wind and rain were showing off their power to each other, and both of them were drenched in the rain like drowned chickens. "Is this society treating us too cruelly?" Meng'ou uttered this painful cry. Qiao Jie comforted him and said, "Meng'ou, don't be discouraged, the future is still there, we should work hard." "Then please come and live with us!" But Qiao declined and said, "Thank you, I'm used to wandering now. Having a fixed place makes me feel annoyed. Goodbye!" Saying that, he carried a bag of clothes and went forward in the wind and rain.

When Meng'ou stared at Qiao Jie's gradually diminishing back, two people approached Meng'ou and asked, "Mr. Lin, long time no see. We've been looking for you everywhere. It's such a coincidence that we met... Our newspaper office is short of an editor and would like to invite you to take on the position..." Meng'ou went with them.

The wind and rain did not stop exerting its power, while on the other side, Suqiu was crying and her sick child was constantly shouting in his mouth with a weak voice, "The sound of the car is ringing, Dad brought the car back."

Meng'ou followed those two people to the newspaper office, met the editor-in-chief, and agreed to give Meng'ou an editing fee of 150 yuan per month, but the prerequisite was that Meng'ou first write an article on selling the country, because this newspaper office had a background. But although Meng'ou was poor and unemployed, he refused to betray the country for personal gain and willingly be a traitor. He firmly refused to agree.

Meng'ou's child died in the thirst for his father to bring a car like Xiao Rong's, and when Suqiu's hand touched his beloved son's nostrils and stopped breathing, she was shocked as if she had lost something, opening her mouth, permanently opening her mouth. She didn't cry, didn't cry loudly, and didn't cry softly, but the tears that followed from her eyes were bright red blood!

Meng'ou came out of the newspaper office, on the way home in the wind and rain, his clothes were wet, dragging his student's footsteps, the sound "da ta, da ta" rang, his face lost the smile of a living person, the dead man looked terrible!

"Graduation is unemployment, how many pounds does a diploma sell for?" This is the central issue of "Elegy of Life." (End)
